{\*\generator Msftedit 5.41.15.1507;}\viewkind4\uc1\pard\f0\fs18 Event Timer 3600\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:ArrayReset\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsLoaded(#Temp) <> 0\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_Mom", #GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_Mom") + 100\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #MaxUsers\par
GoTo ArrayReset\par
EndIf\par
If #NoobBot <> 1\par
If #TrainersNum > 0\par
/Set #TempD, #Rand(3,1)\par
If #TempD = 2\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
/SendAll $CheapBotName & ": The Nubs in the server are:"\par
:nOOb\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
If #IsLoaded(#Temp) <> 0\par
/Set $Temp, $Cheap(#Temp)\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
:Nbot\par
If $Mid($Temp,#TempC,1) = "1"\par
/SendAll $CheapBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " is using " & $GetValue("Nbot_" & $Str(#TempC)) & "."\par
/Inc #TempB\par
EndIf\par
If #TempC < 7\par
/Inc #TempC\par
GoTo Nbot\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #MaxUsers\par
If #TempB > 0\par
/Inc #TempA\par
EndIf\par
GoTo nOOb\par
EndIf\par
If #TempA > 0\par
/SendAll $CheapBotName & ": There is/are " & $Str(#TempA) & " Nub/s in the Server."\par
Else\par
/SendAll $CheapBotName & ": Looks like no one is using Nubish tactic's at this moment."\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par
\par
Event Timer 4\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:ExSpam\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsLoaded(#Temp) <> 0\par
/Set #Spammer(#Temp), 0\par
/Inc #Quite(#Temp), -1\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #MaxUsers\par
GoTo ExSpam\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($GetValue("The_Stats_of_TF9BQ4R22WPSC19U7U3LH_are"), 1) <> "5"\par
:LagFreeness\par
Goto LagFreeness\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par
\par
Event Timer 60\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:Fishing\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Str(#Phase(#Temp)) = "81" AND $WildPoke(#Temp) = "" AND $Str(#IsLoaded(#Temp)) <> "0"\par
/Set #TempA, #Rand(100, 1) \par
If #TempA < 40\par
/SendPM #Temp, $RPGBotName & ": You haven't gotten a bite yet. To stop fishing you type !Stop."\par
/SendPM #Temp, $RPGBotName & ": Fishing needs patience..."\par
Else\par
/Set #TempE, #Val($ExtrInfo(#Temp))\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("SpecPoke_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14 ,3))))\par
/Set $TempB, $Right($TempA, #Len($TempA) - #IsIn($TempA, "/"))\par
If $TempA <> ""\par
If $GetValue($ExtraInfo(#Temp) & "_Short") = $Mid($TempA, #IsIn($TempA, "-") + 1, #IsIn($TempA, "/") - #IsIn($TempA, "-") - 1)\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($TempA, #IsIn($TempA, "-") - 2, 2))\par
EndIf\par
If $TempB <> ""\par
If $GetValue($ExtraInfo(#Temp) & "_Short") = $Mid($TempB, #IsIn($TempB, "-") + 1, #IsIn($TempB, "/") - #IsIn($TempB, "-") - 1)\par
If #TempA = 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($TempB, #IsIn($TempB, "-") - 2, 2))\par
Else\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Mid($TempB, #IsIn($TempB, "-") - 2, 2))\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempD, #Rand(100,0)\par
If #TempD < 2\par
/Set #TempD, #Rand(100,0)\par
If #TempD < #TempA + #TempB\par
If #TempD < #TempA\par
/Set $WildPoke(#Temp), $Left($TempA, 3)\par
Else\par
/Set $WildPoke(#Temp), $Left($TempB, 3)\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Temp, $RPGBotName & ": You got a bite! Do you want to pull? Type !Yes or !No to Answer."\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
EndIf\par
If #TempC = 1\par
If #Day = 1\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetValue($ExtraInfo(#Temp) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14 ,3))))\par
EndIf\par
If #Day = 2\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetValue($ExtraInfo(#Temp) & "_Short") & "_N_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14 ,3))))\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempB, ""\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Len($TempA) / 5\par
/Set #TempF, 0 \par
:FishPercent\par
/Inc #TempF\par
/Set #TempD, #Val($Mid($TempA,#Val(5 * #TempF) - 4,3))\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("Fishing_" & $Str(#TempE)), "," & $Str(#TempD) & ",") > 0\par
/Set $TempB, $TempB & $Mid($TempA,#Val(5 * #TempF) - 4,5)\par
/Set #TempC, #TempC + #Val($Mid($TempA,#Val(5 * #TempF) - 1,2))\par
/Inc #TempB\par
EndIf\par
If #TempF < #TempA\par
GoTo FishPercent\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, #Rand(#TempC, 1)\par
/Set #TempH, 1\par
/Set #TempG, 1\par
/Set #TempD, 1\par
:FishingPerc\par
If #TempG > 1\par
/Set #TempH, #TempH + #TempF - #TempD\par
/Set #TempD, 0\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempF, #Val($Mid($TempB,#Val(5 * #TempG) - 1,2))\par
If #TempA >= #TempH AND #TempA <= #TempH + #TempF\par
/Set $WildPoke(#Temp), $Mid($TempB,#Val(5 * #TempG) - 4,3)\par
/SendPM #Temp, $RPGBotName & ": You got a bite! Do you want to pull? Type !Yes or !No to Answer."\par
Else\par
If #TempG < #TempB\par
/Inc #TempG\par
GoTo FishingPerc\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #MaxUsers\par
GoTo Fishing\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par

Event Timer 120\par
If $Right($Kurts, 1) = "1"\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($Kurts, 26, 2))\par
If #Temp - 2 < 2\par
/SendAll "Kurt: A new batch of my Pok\'e9Balls has just finished!"\par
/Set $Kurts, $Left($Kurts, 27) & "0"\par
Else\par
/Set $Kurts, $Left($Kurts, 25) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Temp - 2), 2) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($RessurectOne, 24, 2))\par

/Set $RessurectOne, $Left($RessurectOne, 25) & "0"\par
Else\par
/Set $RessurectOne, $Left($RessurectOne, 23) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Temp - 2), 2) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($RessurectTwo, 24, 2))\par

/Set $RessurectTwo, $Left($RessurectTwo, 25) & "0"\par
Else\par
/Set $RessurectTwo, $Left($RessurectTwo, 23) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Temp - 2), 2) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Right($RessurectThree, 1) = "1"\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($RessurectThree, 24, 2))\par
If #Temp - 2 < 2\par
/SendAll "Scientist: A Pok\'e9mon has just been ressurected in the RustBoro Laboratory!"\par
/Set $RessurectThree, $Left($RessurectThree, 25) & "0"\par
Else\par
/Set $RessurectThree, $Left($RessurectThree, 23) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Temp - 2), 2) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Tourney = 1\par
/Inc #TourneyStart, - 1\par
If #TourneyStart > 0\par
/Inc #TourneyMes\par
If #TourneyMes = 2\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament is running."\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Please register if you want to participate by using !Reg, and !TourComs to view your other options."\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": There have been " & $Str(#TourneyMems) & " registration out of a maximum of " & $Str(#TourneyMax) & "!"\par
/Set #Temp, #Int(#TourneyStart/30)\par
/Set #TempA, (#TourneyStart - (#Temp*30)) * 2\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": You still have exactly " & $Str(#Temp) & " hours and " & $Str(#TempA) & " minutes left for registration."\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set #TourneyMes, 0\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament has just begun."\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Registrations are now closed!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": There have been " & $Str(#TourneyMems) & " registrations out of a maximum of " & $Str(#TourneyMax) & "!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": It is going to be held with your RPG Status OFF! And in the Room : All for All Arena!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": To know all available commands use !TourComs."\par
If #TourneyMems < 2\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Not enough people in the Tournament! The Tournament is automatically cancelled!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set #Tourney, 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TourneyMax, #TourneyMems\par
GoTo RoundCheck\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #Tourney > 1\par
/Inc #TourneyMes\par
If #TourneyMes = 2\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament is going on, its in round " & $Str(#Tourney-1) & "!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": There are " & $Str(#TourneyMems) & " members who are still in the Tournament out of " & $Str(#TourneyMax) & " players!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": To view the current standings use !TStats, and use !TourComs to view your other options!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set #TourneyMes, 0\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:TourneyLate\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#Temp*21) + (#Temp-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) \par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempA)\par
If #PNumber($TempB) = 0 AND $Mid($TempC, 4, 1) <> "3"\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($TempC, 3, 1))\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #TempA > 4\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": " & $TempB & " has been automatically disqualified because of absense."\par
/Inc #TourneyMems, - 1\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($TempC,5,2))\par
If $Mid($TempC, 4, 1) = "2"\par
:Disq\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), ""\par
If $GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA + 1)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA + 1)) \par
/Inc #TempA\par
GoTo Disq\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #TourneyMatch, - 1\par
Else\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA)),$Left($TempC, 2)) = 1\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $Right($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA)),2)\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA)),2)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($GetValue("TourneyMems"), #Val(#Val($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA))) * 21) +  #Val(#Val($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA))) - 21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempD)\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempD) & " has automatically qualified for the next round!"\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempD, $Left($TempE, 3) & "200"\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempA, $Left($TempC, 3) & "300"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempA, $Left($TempC, 2) & $Str(#TempA) & $Right($TempC, 3)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMax\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo TourneyLate\par
EndIf\par
GoTo RoundCheck\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo Skip\par
:RoundCheck\par
If #Tourney = 1\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:StartVal\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right("0" & $Str(#Temp), 2) & ","\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMems\par
GoTo StartVal\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Tourney, 2\par
/Set #Temp, #TourneyMems\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:Round\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),"-") > 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo Round\par
EndIf\par
If #TourneyMatch = 1\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TourneyMatch_1")\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " has just won the " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament, Congratulations!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_TPoints_of_" & $TempA & "_are")\par
/SaveValue "The_TPoints_of_" & $TempA & "_are", $Left($Temp, (#TourneyType * 2) - 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp, (#TourneyType * 2) - 1, 2)) + 1), 2) & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TourneyType * 2))\par
/SendPM #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)), $BotName & ": You earned 25 Tokens!"\par
/SaveValue $TempA & "_Tokens", #GetValue($TempA & "_Tokens") + 25\par
/Set #Tourney, 0\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/Inc #Tourney\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": The " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament has just entered Round " & $Str(#Tourney-1) & "!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": There are " & $Str(#TourneyMems) & " members who are still in the Tournament out of " & $Str(#TourneyMax) & " players!"\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:WinVal\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right("0" &$GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)), 2) & ","\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo WinVal\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #TourneyMatch\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:Dele\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If $GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), ""\par
If #TempA < 32\par
GoTo Dele\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Randomizing Tournament Match Brackets ......."\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:RandomMatch\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempA & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempB & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempA)*21) + (#Val($TempA)-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $TempB & "-" & $TempA\par
/Set #TourneyMatch, #TempA\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempD)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempD, $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempE)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempE, $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
If #Temp > 1\par
GoTo RandomMatch\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A random player is given a Bye to the next round because of the lack of an opponent!"\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($TempC,2)\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Left($TempC,2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempB*21) + (#TempB-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempA)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempA, $Left($TempB, 3) & "2" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2) \par
/Set #TourneyMatch, #TempA\par
EndIf\par
GoTo ShowBracket\par
:ShowBracket\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Match bracket listings are as follows..."\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:TourneyMatchShow\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)), "-") > 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Right($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21)+(#TempA-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21)\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)\par
EndIf\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)) = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
Else\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)))\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21)) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
GoTo TourneyMatchShow\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Exit\par
:Skip\par
EndEvent\par

If #ShutDown = 1\par

If #Message = 0\par

/Exit\par
Else\par

/Inc #Killsp\par
/Inc #Kills\par

Else\par

/Inc #Killss\par

Else\par

/Inc #Killst\par
/Inc #Kills\par

Else\par

/Inc #Rapes\par
/Set $Temp, $Pokemon(#Rand(389,1))\par
/SendAll $BotName & ": " & $Temp & " just commited a rape on a poor innocent " & $Pokemon(#Rand(389, 1)) & ", bad bad " & $Temp & "!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #DayT < 12\par
/Inc #DayT, +1\par
/Exit\par

/Set #Day, 1\par

Else\par
/Set #Day, 2\par

EndIf\par
If #CSRegn > 0\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE($GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": The " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship is currently running."\par

/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par

/Set #TempB, 0\par
:SpcCmdPoke\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45),3)) = 79 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 6,3)) <> 113 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 3,3)) > 36\par

EndIf\par
:SpcCmdMove\par
/Inc #TempC\par
/Set #TempD, #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 8 + (#TempC * 2) + (#TempC - 2),3))\par

/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),20)\par
EndIf\par

EndIf\par

GoTo SpcCmdPoke\par

EndIf\par

EndIf\par

EndIf\par

/Set $Cheap(#Source), $Left($Cheap(#Source), 6) & "1"\par
Else\par
/Set $Cheap(#Source), $Left($Cheap(#Source), 6) & "0"\par
EndIf\par
If #NoobBot <> 1 \par
/Set $Temp, $Cheap(#Source)\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:Nbot\par
If $Mid($Temp,#Temp,1) = "1"\par
/SendAll $CheapBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " is using " & $GetValue("Nbot_" & $Str(#Temp)) & "."\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 7\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo Nbot\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
If $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR) <> $NewEXTR(#Source)\par
/Set $OrigEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
If $Right($TempA,1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your RPG Status is turned off! To turn it on type !RPGSwitch"\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Type '!Options' to view the server's options list."\par
If $GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#Source) & "_is") = ""\par
/SaveValue "The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#Source) & "_is", $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "00"\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RoomBotName & ": You are now located at: " & $Msg(#Rooms(#Source)) \par
If $Mid($Temp, 14, 1) <> "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $LadderBotName & ": Your Ladder System has been turned on if you want to disable your ladder system type !Ladder Off."\par
/SendPM #Source, $LadderBotName & ": You currently have " & $Mid($Temp, 15, 4) & " Ladder Points."\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, $OrigEXTR(#Source) & "\'abLadder Points:" & $Mid($Temp, 15, 4) & "\'bb \'abTokens:" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Tokens") & "\'bb"\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $LadderBotName & ": Your Ladder System has been turned off if you want to enable your ladder system type !Ladder On."\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, $OrigEXTR(#Source) & "\'abTokens:" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Tokens") & "\'bb"\par
EndIf\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
/SendPM #Source, $StreakBotName & ": Your current Streak is " & $Mid($Temp, 3, 2) & " Consecutive Win(s)."\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
If $Mid($Temp, 7, 1) <> "0"\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are_its_Extra")\par
If $Mid($Temp, 14, 1) <> "0"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, $Mid($TempB, #Val($Mid($Temp, 9, 2)) + 2, #Val($Mid($Temp, 11, 2))) & "\'abLadder Points:" & $Mid($Temp, 15, 4) & "\'bb \'abTokens:" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Tokens") & "\'bb"\par
Else\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, $Mid($TempB, #Val($Mid($Temp, 9, 2)) + 2, #Val($Mid($Temp, 11, 2))) & "\'abTokens:" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Tokens") & "\'bb"\par
EndIf\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($Temp, 13, 1) <> "0" AND #Val($Mid($Temp, 13, 1)) < 3\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#Source) & "_is_its_Poke")\par
:PokeCheck\par
If #HasPoke(#Source, #Val($Mid($TempB, #Temp, 3))) = 1 \par
/Inc #TempB\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #Temp, 3\par
If #Temp < #Len($TempB)\par
Goto PokeCheck\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#Source) & "_is_its_Move")\par
:MoveCheck\par
If #HasPokeMove(#Source, #Val($Mid($TempB, #Temp, 3)), #Val($Mid($TempB, #Temp + 3, 3))) = 1\par
/Inc #TempB\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #Temp, 6\par
If #Temp < #Len($TempB)\par
Goto MoveCheck\par
Else\par
If #TempB > 0\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp, 12) & "0" & $Right($TempB, 9)\par
/Set #Control(#Source), 1 \par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": You have a Pok\'e9mon that you have from your challenges. You can't do that."\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": As a result, your control option has been set to allow."\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": In order to be able to change your control option, you need to change the " & $Str(#TempB) & " Pok\'e9mon that violate your rules."\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($Temp, 8, 1) <> "0"\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are_its_Extra")\par
If $GetValue("Last_Alert_Name_of" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Was") <> $Name(#Source)\par
/SendAll "*** EVERYONE ATTENTION! ***"\par
/SendAll "ALERT: Geuss who's hiding under the Identity of " & $Name(#Source) & ", its none other than the Infamous Alerted Player " & $GetValue("Last_Alert_Name_of" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Was") & "!"\par
/SaveValue "Last_Alert_Name_of" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Was", $Name(#Source)\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "*** EVERYONE ATTENTION! ***"\par
/SendAll "ALERT: " & $Name(#Source) & " is " & $Right($TempB, #Len($TempB) - #Val($Mid($Temp, 9, 2)) - #Val($Mid($Temp, 11, 2))) \par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("AllGLs"), "," & $Name(#Source) & ",") > 0\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 1\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:GymLeader\par
If #TempA = 0\par
/Inc #Temp\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Lead")\par
If #IsIn($Temp,"and") > 0\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #TempA = 1\par
/Set $TempA, $Right($Temp, #IsIn($Temp,"and") - 2)\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($Temp, #Len($Temp) - #Val(#IsIn($Temp,"and") + 3))\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $Temp\par
EndIf\par
If $Name(#Source) = $TempA\par
/Set #GL(#Source), #Temp\par
Else\par
If #Temp < 28\par
GoTo GymLeader\par
If #TempA = 2\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, "Mew's Shrine GymLeader Info" & $Chr(13) & $GetValue("Region_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_Reg")) & "'s " & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_Loc") & " Gym Leader"\par
/Set #Temp, #GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_MLC")\par
/Set #TempA, #GetPokeLevel(#Source,1) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source,2) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source,3) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source,4) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source,5) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source,6)\par
If #TempA > #Temp \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You MLC(Maximum Level Count) is " & $Str(#Temp) & " and your Team exceeds it, All your Pok\'e9mon Levels can't add up to more than it."\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
GoTo InvalidGL\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_MPL")\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:MPL\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #GetPokeLevel(#Source, #TempA) > #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#Source,#TempA)) & "'s Level Exceeds the MPL Limit, Your MPL is " & $Str(#Temp) & " so you can't have a Pok\'e9mon with a higher Level."\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
GoTo InvalidGL\par
EndIf\par
If #TempA < 6\par
GoTo MPL\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:GymTeam\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #IsIn($Temp,$Right("00" & $Str(#GetTeamPoke(#Source, #TempA)) & ",", 3)) > 0\par
If #TempA < 6\par
GoTo GymTeam\par
Else\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 1\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#Source, #TempA)) & " can't be used for this Gym Leader's Pok\'e9mon."\par
EndIf\par
:InvalidGL\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR) & $Chr(13) & "Team Validity = " & $GetValue("GValid_" & $Str(#Valid(#Source))) & "."\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You can access Gym Leader commands using !GLCommands."\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
If #Valid(#Source) = 1\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": Everyone " & $Name(#Source) & " the Gym Leader of " & $GetValue("Region_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_Reg")) & "'s " & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Source)) & "_Loc") & " is ready to accept challenges!"\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
If $Left($TempA,1) = "1"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your RPG Status is turned on! To turn it off type !RPGSwitch"\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), "000000000000000000000"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:SpcCmdPoke\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45),3)) = 79 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 6,3)) <> 113 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 3,3)) > 36\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),20) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
:SpcCmdMove\par
/Inc #TempC\par
/Set #TempD, #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 8 + (#TempC * 2) + (#TempC - 2),3))\par
If #TempD = 39\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),20)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 217\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),1) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),19)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 245\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),2) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),18)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 246\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),3) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),17)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 168\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),4) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),16)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 208\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),5) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),15)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 71\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),6) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),14)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 271\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),7) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),13)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 43\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),13) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),7)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 227\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),14) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),6)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 72\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),15) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),5)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 88\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),16) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),4)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempC < 4\par
GoTo SpcCmdMove\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB < 6\par
GoTo SpcCmdPoke\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:SpecIts\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2) <> "00"\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) > 1 AND #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) < 7\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) \par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),#TempA + 6) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source), 20 - (#TempA + 6))\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 58\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),17) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),3)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2) <> "00"\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 11\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),18) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),2)\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 84\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),19) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),1)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo SpecIts\par
EndIf\par
If #Auth(#Source) > 3\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Administrators have authority on running championships."\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your current championship mode is : " & $GetValue("Region_" & $Str(#RegionMode(#Source))) & "."\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Cash(#Source), #Val($Mid($TempA, 6, 6))\par
/Set #Health(#Source), #Val($Mid($TempA, 3, 3))\par
/Set $Area(#Source), $GetValue("Area_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 14, 3))))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": To check your possible commands type !MainMenu" \par
/Set $Extrinfo(#Source), " LifePoints: " & $Str(#Health(#Source)) & " | Area: " & $Area(#Source) & " | Badges: " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 12, 2))) & " | Cash: $" & $Str(#Cash(#Source)) & "]." & $OrigEXTR(#Source) \par
If $Name(#Source) = "Mew Master" OR $Name(#Source) = "Lord Meshadieme" OR $Name(#Source) = "Lamel"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, "[Creator of this RPG - " & $Extrinfo(#Source)  \par
Else \par
If $Name(#Source) = "Bikaben"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, "[Host of this RPG - " & $Extrinfo(#Source) \par
Else\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, "[Mew's RPG Player - " & $Extrinfo(#Source) \par
EndIf \par
EndIf\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
If $Right($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes"),45) = "000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000"\par
/Set #Team(#Source), 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized but not full yet so you can't battle."\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized and full so your team will now be validated."\par
/Set #Team(#Source), 1\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:PokeChecker\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #GetTeamPoke(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " in position " & $Str(#Temp) & " in our records. You don't have it in your team, the wrong Pok\'e9mon is " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#Source,#Temp)) & ". Remake your team to match our records!"\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #GetPokeLevel(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 3,3))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " is not at Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 3,3))) & "!" \par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6,3)) > 412 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6,3)) < 475\par
If #GetPokeItem(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 7,2)) \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " doesn't have the item " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6, 1) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 7,2)))) & " with it!" \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #GetPokeItem(#Source, #Temp) <> 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " doesn't have the item (No Item) with it!" \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:MoveChecker\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #HasPokeMove(#Source, #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3)), #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempA * 2) + (#TempA - 2),3)) ) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:MoveChecks\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
:MoveChecking\par
/Inc #TempC\par
If #GetPokeMove(#Source,#Temp,#TempB) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempC * 2) + (#TempC - 2),3)) \par
If #TempC < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecking\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " has the move " & $Move(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempA * 2) + (#TempA - 2),3))) & " in our record, but you don't have it in your team! The wrong move is " & $Move(#GetPokeMove(#Source,#Temp,#TempB)) & "!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #TempB < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecks\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #TempA < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecker\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 6\par
GoTo PokeChecker\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 1 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized, full and valid so you can battle now." \par
EndIf\par
Else \par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Hey," & $Name(#Source) & " this is your first time here, isn't it?..Or you might have not initialized your team in your last visit." \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Thats why you have not made your RPG team." \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Just type !Start (ONLY !START), then choose a starter Pok\'e9mon from the list, and to access your options type !MainMenu" \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": If your new and don't understand this type !Help." \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Initialize your team now and don't miss out on the FUN!"\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par
\par
Event -ChatMessage\par
/Set #NoCmd(#Source), 0\par
If #Auth(#Source) = 5\par
If $Left($Message, 11) = "/SaveValue " OR $Left($Message, 11) = "!SaveValue " \par
/StopEvent\par
/Set $SaveValue, $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 11)\par
If #IsIn($SaveValue, ",") = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Invalid format! format is : /SaveValue ValName, Val  "\par
Else\par
/Set #SVTemp, #IsIn($SaveValue, ",") -1\par
If #Len($SaveValue) = #SVTemp + 1\par
/SaveValue $Left($SaveValue, #SVTemp), ""\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": A blank value has been saved to '" & $Left($SaveValue, #SVTemp) & "'!"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $Left($SaveValue, #SVTemp), $Right($SaveValue,#Len($SaveValue) - #SVTemp - 2)\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": The value '" & $Right($SaveValue,#Len($SaveValue) - #SVTemp - 2) & "' has been saved to '" & $Left($SaveValue, #SVTemp) & "'!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Message, 11) = "/ShowValue " OR $Left($Message, 11) = "!ShowValue "\par
/StopEvent\par
/Set $SaveValue, $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 11)\par
If $GetValue($SaveValue) = ""\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Value does not exist thus the value '" & $SaveValue & "' is empty!"\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": The value '" & $SaveValue & "' is : '" & $GetValue($SaveValue) & "'."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Message, 4) = "****"\par
/StopEvent\par
/Inc #Spammer(#Source)\par
GoTo Spamming\par
EndIf\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 98\par
/StopEvent\par
If $Message = "!Cancel" Or $Message = "/Cancel"\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Prompt Exited. You may now use the Main Chat again."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
Else\par
If $Message = $Left($GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are_its_Extra"), #Val($Mid($GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are"), 9, 2)))\par
/Set #Auth(#Source), #Val($Left($GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_are"), 1))\par
If #Auth(#Source) = 2\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, AUTH, 1 \par
Else \par
If #Auth(#Source) > 2\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, AUTH, 2 \par
EndIf \par
EndIf \par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": You have Successfully Logged In as a authority figure."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Incorrect Password! Please retry or type !Cancel to quit this prompt situation."\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 99\par
/StopEvent\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 AND #Val($Message) > 8\par

EndIf\par

Else\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp, 25, 1)) < 3\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " is not banned from using Controls."\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp, 24) & "0" & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 25)\par
/SendAll $BotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " is now allowed to use Controls again."\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 9) = "EditInfo " \par
/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 9))\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 9) \par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Type in what you want in " & $Name(#Temp) & "'s info. Type !Cancel to stop changing this person's info." \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 2\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 7) = "UnEdit " OR $Left($Cmd, 7) = "DeEdit "\par
/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 7))\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Temp, EXTR, $OrigEXTR(#Temp) & "\'abTokens:" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_Tokens") & "\'bb"\par

/Exit\par

EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par

/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": You don't have the authority to take " & $Name(#Temp) & " off Alert."\par

Else\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_are")\par

/SendAll $BotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " has been taken off Alert." \par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 10))\par
If #Auth(#Source) < #Val($Mid($GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_are"), 8, 1)) AND #Auth(#Source) <> 5\par

If $Left($Cmd, 4) = "*** " \par
/Inc #Spammer(#Source)\par

:ShowPoke\par

Else\par

EndIf\par

EndIf\par

Else\par
/Set $Temp, $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 4)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($Temp, #IsIn($Temp, ",") - 1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - #IsIn($Temp, ","))\par

/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempC, ""\par

EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $BotName & ": Invalid command! Use !Options to find what you can use!"\par

/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command!"\par
/Exit\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You are not in a prompt situation."\par

EndIf\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Flying"),#GetValue("Fly_" & $GetValue("Area_"& $Str(#Temp))),1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You haven't gone to " & $GetValue("Area_"& $Str(#Temp)) & " yet so your Pok\'e9mon does not know the way to go so you cant go until you go by foot!" \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " is riding a flying Pok\'e9mon to " & $GetValue("Area_"& $Str(#Temp)) & "."\par
/Set #TempF, #Health(#Source) - #Rand(15,2)\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
If #TempF < 1\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($Temp, 2) & "000" & $Mid($Temp,6,8) & $Right("00" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_LastPCCity"),3) & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 16) \par
/Set $Area(#Source), $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_LastPC")\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": That was awful you were soo tired that you fainted and a mysterious person brought you to the Pok\'e9mon Center you last visited."\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " fainted due to starvation and was found in a Pok\'e9mon Center! And you call yourself a Pok\'e9mon Trainer, shame on you!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
GoTo NewInfoIn\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($Temp, 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempF), 3) & $Mid($Temp,6,8) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Temp), 3) & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 16)\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You returned your Pok\'e9mon and are now in " & $GetValue("Area_"& $Str(#Temp)) & "!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 8\par
If #PNumber($Trader(#Source)) = 0 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Trader(#Source) & " is not on the server anymore so you can't trade with them."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Message) > 0 AND #Val($Message) < 7\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Mid($Temp,(#Val($Message)*45) + (#Val($Message)-45),45) & ","\par
/Set $TradePoke(#Source), $Temp\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesOT")\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Mid($TempA, #IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message) - 1)) + 2,(#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message)))) - (#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message) - 1)) + 2))\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 9\par
/Set #TradeNo(#Source), #Val($Message)\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want from " & $Trader(#Source) & ". You can type !CancelTrade to exit the prompt."\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:TradeMsg\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#Temp*45) + (#Temp-45),45)\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,4,3))) & "."\par
If #Temp < 6 \par
GoTo TradeMsg\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": That is not a valid command. Please type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to trade or type !CancelTrade to exit the prompt."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 9\par
If #PNumber($Trader(#Source)) = 0 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Trader(#Source) & " is not on the server anymore so you can't trade with them."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Message) > 0 AND #Val($Message) < 7\par
/Set $Temp, $TradePoke(#Source)\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($Temp,4,3))\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Mid($Temp,(#Val($Message)*45) + (#Val($Message)-45),45) & ","\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($Temp,4,3))\par
If #Phase(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))) <> 12\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry but you can't trade with " & $Trader(#Source) & " because s/he left the Pok\'e9mon Center!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #TempA <> #Temp\par
If #TempA > #Temp\par
If #TempA - #Temp > 10\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry but you can't trade with a level difference above 10!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #Temp - #TempA > 10\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry but you can't trade with a level difference above 10!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), $Temp\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_PokesOT")\par
/Set $EditInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), $Mid($TempA, #IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message) - 1)) + 2,(#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message)))) - (#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Val($Message) - 1)) + 2))\par
/Set #TradeNt(#Source), #Val($Message)\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The trade request has been sent to " & $Trader(#Source) & ". The trade is for your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#Source),3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TradePoke(#Source),4,3))) & ", for his/her " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))),3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))),4,3))) & ". You can type !CancelTrade to cancel the trade. If one of you disconnect the trade cancels."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 10\par
/Set #Phase(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 11\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), ""\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), "*** ATTENTION YOU HAVE A TRADE REQUEST ***"\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " has sent you a trade request for your " & $Pokemon($Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))),3)) & " at Lv " & $Str($Mid($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))),4,3)) & ", for his/her " & $Pokemon($Left($TradePoke(#Source),3)) & " at Lv " & $Str($Mid($TradePoke(#Source),4,3)) & ". Please type !Accept or !Decline to answer. If one of you disconnect the trade cancels."\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), ""\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": That is not a valid command. Please type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to trade or type !CancelTrade to exit the prompt."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 10\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Remember you have a pending trade with " & $Trader(#Source) & "! You can type !CancelTrade to exit the prompt."\par
GoTo Spamming\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 11\par
If $Message <> "!Accept" AND $Message <> "!Decline" AND $Message <> "/Accept" AND $Message <> "/Decline"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your trade request from " & $Trader(#Source) & " is still pending. Please type !Accept or !Decline to answer."\par
GoTo Spamming\par
Else\par
If $Message = "!Decline" OR $Message = "/Decline" \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Set #Phase(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 12\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your trade has been canceled!"\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": Your trade has been declined!"\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If $Message = "!Accept" OR $Message = "/Accept" \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have accepted the trade!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your Pok\'e9mon are being traded......"\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " has accepted the trade!"\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": Your Pok\'e9mon are being traded......"\par
/Set #TempA, #PNumber($Trader(#Source))\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($TradePoke(#TempA),8,2))\par
:TradeEvo\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & "_Trade_" & $Str(#Temp)) <> ""\par
If $Mid($TradePoke(#TempA),7,1) = "4" XOR #Temp = 0\par
If #TempA = #Source\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & " is trying to evolve into " & $Pokemon(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & "_Trade_" & $Str(#Temp))) & ", please type !Pokemon to find out how to evolve it."\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & " is trying to evolve into " & $Pokemon(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & "_Trade_" & $Str(#Temp))) & ", please type !Pokemon to find out how to evolve it."\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TradePoke(#TempA), $Left($TradePoke(#TempA), #Len($TradePoke(#TempA)) - 4) & $Right("00" & $Str(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#TempA),3))) & "_Trade_" & $Str(#Temp))), 3) & ","\par
If #Temp <> 0\par
/Set $TradePoke(#TempA), $Left($TradePoke(#TempA),6) & "100" & $Right($TradePoke(#TempA),#Len($TradePoke(#TempA) - 9)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #TempA = #PNumber($Trader(#Source))\par
/Set #TempA, #Source\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($TradePoke(#TempA),8,2))\par
GoTo TradeEvo\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_PokesOT")\par
/Set #Temp, #TradeNo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)))\par
If #Temp = 6\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_Pokes", $Left($Temp,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45)-1) & $Left($TradePoke(#Source), 45)\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_Pokes", $Left($Temp,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45)-1) & $TradePoke(#Source) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - (((#Temp+1)*45)+((#Temp+1)-45)-1))\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_PokesOT", $Left($TempA,#IsIn($TempA, "*" & $Str(#Temp-1)) + 1) & $EditInfo(#Source) & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - (#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Temp-1)) + 1 + #Len($EditInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))))))\par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_Pokedex"), "," & $Right($TradePoke(#Source), 3) & ",") = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Pokedex")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Pokedex", $TempB & $Right($TradePoke(#Source), 3) & ","\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($TempB,20) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB, 18, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 23)\par
EndIf\par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)), PSID) & "_Seen_Poke"), "," & $Left($TradePoke(#Source), 3) & ",") = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Seen_Poke")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_Seen_Poke", $TempB & $Left($TradePoke(#Source), 3) & ","\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)),PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($TempB,20) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB, 21, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 23)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_PokesOT")\par
/Set #Temp, #TradeNt(#PNumber($Trader(#Source)))\par
If #Temp = 6\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokes", $Left($Temp,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45)-1) & $Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 45)\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokes", $Left($Temp,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45)-1) & $TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - (((#Temp+1)*45)+((#Temp+1)-45)-1))\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_PokesOT", $Left($TempA,#IsIn($TempA, "*" & $Str(#Temp-1)) + 1) & $EditInfo(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))) & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - (#IsIn($TempA,"*" & $Str(#Temp-1)) + 1 + #Len($EditInfo(#Source))))\par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokedex"), "," & $Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 3) & ",") = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokedex")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokedex", $TempB & $Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 3) & ","\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($TempB,20) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB, 18, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 23)\par
EndIf\par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Seen_Poke"), "," & $Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 3) & ",") = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Seen_Poke")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Seen_Poke", $TempB & $Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 3) & ","\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($TempB,20) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB, 21, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 23)\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/Set #Phase(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 12\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your Pok\'e9mon have been traded."\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": Your Pok\'e9mon have been traded."\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You will have to make your team again with your new Pok\'e9mon."\par
/SendPM #PNumber($Trader(#Source)), $RPGBotName & ": You will have to make your team again with your new Pok\'e9mon."\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
/Set #Valid(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 0 \par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** ATTENTION  IMPORTANT  ANNOUNCEMENT  FROM  THE  POK\'c9MON  CENTER ***" \par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": A Trade has been completed between " & $Name(#Source) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#Source), 3))) & " at Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TradePoke(#Source), 4, 3))) & " and " & $Trader(#Source) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 3))) & " at Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TradePoke(#PNumber($Trader(#Source))), 4, 3))) & "!"\par
/SendAll ""\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo SpecialCmd\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 12\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
If $Message = "!Back" OR $Message = "/Back"\par
If #Health(#Source) < 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Nurse Joy: Hey! You can't go now! Your too weak to go battle!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "Nurse Joy: Good bye! Hope you come again."\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have exited the Pok\'e9mon Center!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "!Heal" OR $Message = "/Heal"  \par
If #Health(#Source) = 100\par
/SendPM #Source, "Nurse Joy: Your health is full and you are fully refreshed you don't need to heal yourself."\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, "Nurse Joy: Your health was " & $Str(#Health(#Source)) & " Life Points. Now you have been completely healed!"\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($Temp, 2) & "100" & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 5)\par
/Set #Health(#Source), 100\par
GoTo NewInfoIn\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Message, 7) = "!Trade " OR $Left($Message, 7) = "/Trade "\par
/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7)) \par
If #Temp = #Source\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Stop trading with yourself!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 0 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7) & " is not connected to the Server."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Right($Area(#PNumber($Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7))), 3) <> " PC"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7) & " needs to be in a Pok\'e9mon Center before s/he can trade."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Team(#Source) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not full you must have a full team to Trade."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Team(#Temp) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7) & "'s Team is not full s/he must have a full team to trade."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to trade to " & $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7) & ". You can type !CancelTrade to cancel the trade."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 8\par
/Set $Trader(#Source), $Right($Message, #Len($Message) - 7) \par
/Set $Trader(#Temp), $Name(#Source)\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokes") \par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:Trade\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempA,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45),45)\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($TempB,1,3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB,4,3))) & "."\par
If #Temp < 6\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo Trade\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "!PC" OR $Message = "/PC"\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Please choose your options:"\par
/SendPM #Source, "1: Pok\'e9mon Database."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2: Inventory Database."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3: Exit."\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 13\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "!Area" OR $Message = "/Area"\par
GoTo Location\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Message, 1) = "!" OR $Left($Message, 1) = "/"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Nurse Joy: Sorry but you cant carry out any other Commands because you are in the Pok\'e9mon Center."\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/SendAll $Name(#Source) & ": " & $Message\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 13\par
If $Message <> "1" AND $Message <> "2" AND $Message <> "3"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command!"\par
Else\par
If $Message = "3"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have been Disconnected from the PC."\par
GoTo SpecialCmd\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "1"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 14\par
:PokeComp\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Current Box Number is " & $Str(#GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_PC")) & " ."\par
/SendPM #Source, "1:View your Pok\'e9mon in the Box."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2:Change the Current Box Number."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3:Withdraw a Pok\'e9mon from the Database to your Team."\par
/SendPM #Source, "4:Deposit a Pok\'e9mon from your Team to the DataBase."\par
/SendPM #Source, "5:Release a Pok\'e9mon from the Database."\par
/SendPM #Source, "6:Exit"\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "2"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 15\par
:ItemComp\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Please Choose your Options:"\par
/SendPM #Source, "1:View all the Items in the Database."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2:Withdraw an Item from the Database to your BackPack."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3:Deposit an Item from your BackPack to the DataBase."\par
/SendPM #Source, "4:Throw away an Item from the Database."\par
/SendPM #Source, "5:Exit"\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 14\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 6\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command!"\par
Else\par
If $Message = "6"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have been Disconnected from the PC."\par
GoTo SpecialCmd\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "1"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Current Box Number is " & $Str(#GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_PC")) & " ."\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), "1"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 14\par
GoTo ShowBox\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "2"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 19\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Please type the number of the box you want to change to:"\par
GoTo ShowDataBase\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "3"\par
If #Team(#Source) = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: ERROR! Your team is already full!"\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
Else\par
If $Left($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $GetValue($GetPlayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PC") & "Pokes"), 3) = "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: ERROR! Your Pok\'e9monBox is Empty!"\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
Else\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 18\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Please type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to withdraw:"\par
GoTo ShowBox\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Message = "4"\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes"),47,3) = "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: ERROR! Your team has only one Pok\'e9mon you can't remove your last Pok\'e9mon!"\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Right($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $GetValue($GetPlayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PC") & "Pokes"), 45)) <> 0\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: ERROR! Your Pok\'e9monBox is Full!"\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 17\par

GoTo ShowBox\par
EndIf\par

Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 15\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 5\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command!"\par
Else\par

/Set #Phase(#Source), 12\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have been Disconnected from the PC."\par

/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Your Database Items:"\par

/Set #TempD, #IsIn($TempA, "*" & $Str(#Temp+1)) - 1\par
If #TempC = #TempB\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #TempC) & $Mid($TempA, #TempB + 2 + #Len($Str(#Temp)), #TempD - (#TempB + 1 + #Len($Str(#Temp)))) & $Right($TempA, #Len($TempA) - #TempB)\par
If #Temp < 19\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo Release\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue $GetplayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#TempA) & "PokesOT", $TempA\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $GetplayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#TempA) & "Pokes", $Left($Temp, (#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) - 1) & "000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000"\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#TempA) & "PokesOT")\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #IsIn($TempA, "*" & $Str(#Temp-1)) + #Len($Str(#Temp-1))) & "*20"\par
/SaveValue $GetplayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#TempA) & "PokesOT", $TempA\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 24\par
If $Message = "!Menu" OR $Message = "/Menu"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 15\par
GoTo ItemComp\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3) + 2,2))\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command! Type the number of how many " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)))) & " you want to throw."\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"))\par

/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"), $Left($TempA,#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3) - 1) & $Right($TempA,40 - #Val(#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3) + 3)) & "0000"\par

EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have thrown away " & $Message & " " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)))) & " from your Database."\par

/Exit\par

If #Phase(#Source) = 25\par

/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Invalid command! Type the number of how many " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)))) & " you want to withdraw."\par
Else\par

:ItemWithdraw\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 3) + (#Temp - 3), 4) = "0000"\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Item" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"), $Left($Temp,#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) - 1) & $Mid($TempA,#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA), 2) & $Right($Temp,40 - #Val(#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) + 3))\par
Else\par
If $Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 3) + (#Temp - 3),2) = $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)\par

If $Right($Temp,4) <> "0000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Sorry you don't have enough space in your BackPack for that many!"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: How many would you like to withdraw(maximum is 99)? Or type !Menu to go back to Item Database."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, (#TempA + #Val($Mid($Temp,#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) + 2,2))) - 99\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Item" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"), $Left($Temp,#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) + 1) & "99" & $Right($Temp,40 - #Val(#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) + 3))\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Item" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"))\par

EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have withdrawn " & $Message & " " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)))) & " to your BackPack."\par

/SendPM #Source, "Computer: You have Deposited " & $Message & " " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,#Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) * 3) + #Val(#Val($EditInfo(#Source)) - 3),2)))) & " to your Database."\par

Else\par

/Set #Phase(#Source), 27\par
GoTo Location\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 99\par
/SendPM #Source, "Clerk: Invalid command!"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Clerk: How many would you like to buy(maximum is 99)? Or type !Browse to go back to browsing."\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, #Cash(#Source)\par
If #Val($GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $EditInfo(#Source) & "_Price")) * #Val($Message) > #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, "Clerk: Sorry you don't have enough money for " & $Message & " " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $EditInfo(#Source)) & "!"\par

/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#Val($ExtrInfo(#Source)) + 1)\par
GoTo OBOItemBox\par

If #TempA < #Len($TempB) - 1\par
/Inc #TempA, 2\par
GoTo MachCheck\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempC, 3))) & " = NOT ABLE."\par
If #Temp < 6 \par
GoTo MachineMove\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 39\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 39\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 6\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! Type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to teach." \par
Else\par
If #IsIn($EditInfo(#Source),$Message) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! Type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to teach." \par
Else\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Message & "1"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempB, #Val(#Val($Left($EditInfo(#Source),1)) * 45) + #Val(#Val($Left($EditInfo(#Source),1)) - 45)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, #TempB, 45)\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:PrevMach\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #Val($Mid($TempA, 9 + (#Temp*2) + (#Temp-2), 3)) = #Val($ExtrInfo(#Source))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry that Pok\'e9mon already knows the move " & $Move(#Val($ExtrInfo(#Source))) & "! Type the number of the Pok\'e9mon you want to teach." \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 4\par
GoTo PrevMach\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:MachineSlot\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($TempA, 9 + (#Temp*2) + (#Temp-2), 3) = "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Are you sure you want to teach " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " the move " & $Move(#Val($ExtrInfo(#Source))) & ".Type !Yes or !No to answer." \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 37\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $EditInfo(#Source) & $Str(#Temp)\par
Else\par
If #Temp < 4\par
GoTo MachineSlot\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of the move you want to replace to teach " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " the move " & $Move(#Val($ExtrInfo(#Source))) & "."\par
/Set #Temp, 0 \par
:MachineSlots\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempA,9 + #Val(#Val(#Temp*2) + #Val(#Temp-2)),3))) & "."\par
If #Temp < 4 \par
GoTo MachineSlots\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 36\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 40\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > #Val($ExtrInfo(#Source))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! Type the number of the evolutionary stone you want to use." \par

/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemk")\par

/Set #TempB, #Val(#Temp * 45) + #Val(#Temp - 45)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, #TempB, 45)\par

If #Temp < 6\par
GoTo StonePoke\par
EndIf\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#TempA)\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 41\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! That is not a evolutionary stone, please try again." \par
EndIf\par

/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 41\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! Pok\'e9mon can't evolve with that stone." \par

If #Phase(#Source) = 42\par

Else\par

/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), 100\par
/Set #WildPoke(#Source), 100\par
/Set #TeamSt(#Source), 1\par
/Set #WildSt(#Source), 1\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 52\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 5\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Sorry invalid number! Type the number of what you want to do." \par
Else\par
If $Message = "1"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of the move you want to use on the Wild Pok\'e9mon."\par
/Set #Temp, 4\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:WildAttack\par
/Inc #Temp, + 3\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#TempA) & ": " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TeamPoke(#Source),#Temp,3))) & "."\par
If #TempA < 4\par
GoTo WildAttack\par
EndIf \par
/Inc #TempA\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#TempA)\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#TempA) & ": Back."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 53\par
Else\par
If $Message = "2"\par
If #Team(#Source) = 1 \par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Box" & $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PC") & "Pokes"), "000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000") = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You can't catch a Pok\'e9mon your team and box Pok\'e9mon are full!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of what you want to do." \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Itemb") = "0000000000000000000000000000000000000000"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You can't catch a Pok\'e9mon because you don't have any Pok\'e9ball's." \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of what you want to do." \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Please type the number of the ball you want to use to try and catch the Wild Pok\'e9mon."\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:WildBall\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemb"),#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3),2) <> ""\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemb"),#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3),2) <> "00"\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $GetValue("Item_b_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemb"),#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3),2))) ) & " = " & $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemb"),#Val(#Temp * 3) + #Val(#Temp - 3) + 2,2)\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo WildBall\par
Else\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#Temp+1)\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#Temp)\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#Temp)\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $ExtrInfo(#Source) & ": Back."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 54\par
Else\par
If $Message = "3"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": What do you want to throw?"\par
/SendPM #Source, "1: Food to keep it from escaping and keeping it occupied."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2: Throw a rock at it to get its attention and/or make it angry."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3: Poke it with a stick and dodge its distracted attack."\par
/SendPM #Source, "4: Back."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 67\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If $Message = "4"\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:WildFlute\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemk"),#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3),2) = "01"\par
If #WildSt(#Source) <> 2 AND #TeamSt(#Source) <> 2\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Both of the Pok\'e9mon are not sleeping there is no use for the Pok\'e9flute."\par
GoTo Battle\par
Else\par
If #WildSt(#Source) = 2\par
/Set #WildSt(#Source), 1\par
EndIf\par
If #TeamSt(#Source) = 2\par
/Set #TeamSt(#Source), 1\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You played your Pok\'e9flute and the sleeping Pok\'e9mon awoke."\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo WildFlute\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You don't have a Pok\'e9flute to use."\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If $Message = "5"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Itemi")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:SmokeBall\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($Temp,#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3),2) = "83"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You threw a smokeball and escaped!"\par
If $Mid($Temp,#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)+2,2) = "01"\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Itemi", $Left($Temp,#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)-1) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - #Val(#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)+3)) & "0000"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Itemi", $Left($Temp,#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)+1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)+2,2)) - 1), 2) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - #Val(#Val(#Temp*3) + #Val(#Temp-3)+3)) \par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo SmokeBall\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($WildPoke(#Source),3) = "050" OR $Left($WildPoke(#Source),3) = "051" OR $Left($WildPoke(#Source),3) = "328" \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Wild Pok\'e9mon is not letting you escape because of its trait Arena Trap."\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
If #Run(#Source) = 6\par

GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($WildPoke(#Source), 4, 3)) -  #Val($Mid($TeamPoke(#Source), 4, 3)) \par
/Set #TempA, #Rand(100,1)\par
If #Temp < 0\par
/Set #TempB, 90\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp > 0 AND #Temp < 5\par
/Set #TempB, 70\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp > 5 AND #Temp < 10 \par
/Set #TempB, 50\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp > 10 AND #Temp < 20\par
/Set #TempB, 40\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp > 20\par
/Set #TempB, 30\par
EndIf\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You escaped from the Wild Pok\'e9mon."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Wild Pok\'e9mon is not letting you escape."\par

EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 53\par

Else\par

/Exit\par
EndIf\par

/Exit\par

/Exit\par

\par
\par

/Set #TempE, #WildSt(#Source) \par
/Set #TempF, #TeamPoke(#Source) \par
/Set #TempG, #WildPoke(#Source) \par
/Set #TempH, #Val($Message)\par
:Turn\par
If #TempD = 3\par
/Set #Temp, #Rand(3,1)\par
If #Temp = 2\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempE & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempC,3))) & " woke up!"\par

Else\par
/Set #WildSt(#Source), 1\par
EndIf\par
Else\par

If $TempC = $TeamPoke(#Source)\par
GoTo WildTurn\par
Else\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #WildSt(#Source), 1\par
EndIf\par

GoTo WildTurn\par
Else\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par

Else\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

If #TempB > #TempG\par
/Set #TempB, #TempG\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempF & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempD,3))) & " lost " & $Str(#TempB) & "% of its health."\par

/Set #WildPoke(#Source), #Int(#WildPoke(#Source) - #TempB)\par
/Set #TempG, #WildPoke(#Source) \par
Else\par
/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), #Int(#TeamPoke(#Source) - #TempB)\par
/Set #TempG, #TeamPoke(#Source) \par
EndIf\par

GoTo Exp\par
Else\par

EndIf\par
EndIf\par

EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), #TeamPoke(#Source) + #Temp\par
If #TeamPoke(#Source) > 100\par
/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), 100\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempG, #TeamPoke(#Source) \par
Else\par
/Set #WildPoke(#Source), #WildPoke(#Source) + #Temp\par

/Set #TempG, #WildPoke(#Source) \par
EndIf\par

GoTo WildTurn\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #TeamSt(#Source) <> 1\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #WildSt(#Source), #TempA\par
/Set #TempE, #WildSt(#Source) \par
GoTo WildTurn\par
Else\par
/Set #TeamSt(#Source), #TempA\par
/Set #TempE, #TeamSt(#Source) \par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par

/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), #TeamPoke(#Source) + #Temp\par
If #TeamPoke(#Source) > 100\par
/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), 100\par

/Set #TempG, #TeamPoke(#Source) \par
Else\par
/Set #WildPoke(#Source), #WildPoke(#Source) + #Temp\par
If #WildPoke(#Source) > 100\par
/Set #WildPoke(#Source), 100\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempG, #WildPoke(#Source) \par
EndIf\par
Else\par

If $GetValue("Move_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC,#Val(#TempH * 3) + 4,3)))  & "_Eff") = "7"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempF & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempD,3))) & " is OHKO'ed!"\par

GoTo Exp\par
Else\par
GoTo WildLose\par
EndIf\par

If #TempE <> 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": But it failed!"\par
If $TempC = $TeamPoke(#Source)\par
GoTo WildTurn\par
Else\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempF & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempD,3))) & " is " & $GetValue("Status_" & $Right($GetValue("Move_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC,(#TempH* 3) + 4,3))) & "_Eff"),1) & "_Full") & "!"\par
If $TempC = $TeamPoke(#Source)\par
/Set #WildSt(#Source), #Val($Right($GetValue("Move_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC,#Val(#TempH* 3) + 4,3))) & "_Eff"),1))\par
GoTo WildTurn\par
Else\par
/Set #TeamSt(#Source), #Val($Right($GetValue("Move_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC,#Val(#TempH* 3) + 4,3))) & "_Eff"),1))\par
GoTo Battle\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If $GetValue("Move_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC,#Val(#TempH * 3) + 4,3))) & "_Eff") = "9"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": But it failed!"\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempE & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempC,3))) & " missed!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $TempC = $TeamPoke(#Source)\par
:WildTurn\par
/Set #Temp, #Rand(4,1)\par
If $Mid($WildPoke(#Source),#Val(#Temp * 3) + 4,3) = "000"\par
GoTo WildTurn\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempC, $WildPoke(#Source)\par
/Set $TempD, $TeamPoke(#Source)\par
/Set $TempF, ""\par
/Set $TempE, "Wild "\par
/Set #TempE, #TeamSt(#Source) \par
/Set #TempD, #WildSt(#Source) \par
/Set #TempF, #WildPoke(#Source) \par
/Set #TempG, #TeamPoke(#Source) \par

GoTo Turn\par
Else\par

EndIf\par

Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 54\par

/Set #Temp, 1.5\par

/Set #Temp, 4.5\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, 1.5\par
Else\par

:Moonball\par

Else\par

/Set #TempD, #Val($Mid($WildPoke(#Source),4,3))\par
If #Temp < 6\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(100, 1)\par
/Set #TempE, 0\par

/Set #TempE, #Round((#TempC-#TempD) / 40, 3)\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Temp * (#TempE + 1.5)\par
If #WildSt(#Source) = 3 OR #WildSt(#Source) = 4\par
/Set #Temp, #Temp * 2\par
Else\par
If #WildSt(#Source) <> 1\par
/Set #Temp, #Temp * 1.5\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempC, #Val($Right($WildPokeState(#Source), 1))\par
/Set #TempD, #Val($Left($WildPokeState(#Source), 1))\par
If #TempC > #TempD\par
/Set #Temp, #Temp * (1 + (#TempC + #TempD / 10))\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, #Temp * (1 - (#TempC + #TempD / 10))\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempA, #Int(#WildPoke(#Source) / 10)\par

/Set #TempA, 0\par
