/SendPM #Source, "Professor " & $GetValue("PLab_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3)))) & ": You have also caught and owned a " & $Message & " before."\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, "Professor " & $GetValue("PLab_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3)))) & ": You still haven't owned a " & $Message & " yet."\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, "Professor " & $GetValue("PLab_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3)))) & ": Looks like you still have to look for a " & $Message & " in the wild."\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "Professor " & $GetValue("PLab_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3)))) & ": What brings you here?"\par
/SendPM #Source, "1: Pok\'e9dex checkup."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2: Check if you have seen or caught a Pok\'e9mon."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3: Buy rare items."\par
/SendPM #Source, "4: Just saying hi and leaving."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 61\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 77\par
If #Val($Message) < 1 OR #Val($Message) > 7\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Invalid number! Please type the number of the range of Pok\'e9mon in the Itemdex."\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, #GetValue("LowerLimit_" & $Str(#Val($Message)) & "_1")\par
If #Val($Message) < 7 \par

Else\par
/Set #TempA, #GetValue("UpperLimit_" & $Str(#Val($Message)) & "_9")\par

GoTo ItemDex\par

Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 78\par

/Exit\par
Else\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Itemk")\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par

/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Invalid number! Please type the number of the fishing rod you want use."\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/Set #Timer(#Source), 0\par

/Set $WildPokeState(#Source), "00"\par

EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 79\par

/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par

/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes") \par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:SalonPoke\par

EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 80\par

Else\par

/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempA, #Val(#Val($Message) * 7) + #Val(#Val($Message) - 7), 7)\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Right($TempB, 2))\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($TempB, 1))\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Mid($TempB, 2, 2))\par

/Set #Temp, #Temp - 2\par

/Set #Temp, #Temp - 1\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, #Temp + 1\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempA, #TempA + 1\par
EndIf\par

/Set #Temp, #TempC\par

/Set #TempA, 9\par

/SendPM #Source, "Salon Maiden: Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp, #Val(#Val($Message) * 45) + #Val(#Val($Message) - 45), 3))) & " looks unhappy."\par
Else\par

/Set $TempB, $Right($TempA, 18)\par

/Inc #TempB\par
/SaveValue $Left($Temp, 21) & "_ChampionShip", $Str(#Temp) & $Right("0" & $Str(#TempD), 2) & "1" & $Str(#TempB) & "00"\par
If #TempB = 1\par
/Set $TempA, $TempA & $Left($Temp, 22)\par
Else\par
If #TempB = 2\par
/Set $TempB, $TempB & $Left($Temp, 22)\par
Else\par
If #TempB = 3\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Left($Temp, 22)\par
Else\par
/Set $TempD, $TempD & $Left($Temp, 22)\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
/Inc #TempD\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 22)\par
If #TempC > 0\par
GoTo BracketSplit\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_1", $TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_2", $TempB\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_3", $TempC\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_4", $TempD\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:OBOReturn\par
If #TempB < 4\par
/Inc #TempB\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round", 1\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match", 0\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Mem", #Len($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))) / 22\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Max", #Len($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))) / 22\par
GoTo OBOCSR\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " chamionship is already running."\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Not enough people registered."\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You don't have a valid region mode."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 3) = "Dq "\par
/Set $TempE, $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 3)\par
/Set #Temp, #RegionMode(#Source)\par
If #CSRegn = 0\par
\f1 /SendPM #Source, $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": The ChampionShip has not started yet."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
\f0 /Set $TempA, $Left($GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $TempE & "_is"), 21)\par
/Set $TempD, $GetValue("ChampionShip_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Registrants")\par
If #IsIn($TempD,$TempA) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempE & " is not in the Championship."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempA & "_Championship")\par
If $Mid($Temp,4,1) = "3"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempE & " has already been disqualified in the Championship!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #CSMems, - 1\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Mid($Temp, 5, 1))\par
/SaveValue "\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempA) & "_Mems",\f0  #GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempC) & "_Mems"\f0 ) - 1\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempA & "_Championship")\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $TempE & " has been disqualified from the " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship by " & $Name(#Source) & "."\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($Temp,6,2))\par
/Set #TempB, #TempA\par
/SaveValue $TempA & "_Championship", $Left($Temp, 3) & "3" & $Str(#TempC) & "00"\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp, 4, 1)) > 3\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempC) & "_Round", "X"\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempC) & "_Match", 0\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": That ends the matches from Tier " & $Str(#TempC) & " of the Championship."\par
Else\par
If $Mid($Temp, 4, 1) = "2"\par
:CSDisq\par
/SaveValue "\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempB)\f0 , ""\par
If $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB + 1)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB), $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB+ 1)) \par
/Inc #TempB\par
GoTo CSDisq\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempC) & "_Match", #GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempC) & "_Match"\f0 ) - 1\par
Else\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB)),$Left($Temp, 2)) = 1\par
/SaveValue "\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB), $Right($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB)),2)\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB), $Left($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB)),2)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC)), #Val(#Val($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB))) * 21) +  #Val(#Val($GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & \f0 $Str(#TempC) \f1 & "_Match_" & \f0 $Str(#TempB))) - 21), 21)\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($TempB & "_Championship")\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & " has automatically qualified for the next round!"\par
/SaveValue $TempB & "_Championship", $Left($TempC, 3) & "2" & $Str(#TempC) & "00"\par
EndIf\par
GoTo OBOCSR\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "CSMems"\par
If #CSRegn > 0\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("ChampionShip_" & $Str(#CSRegn) & "_Registrants")\par
If #CSRegn = 1\par
/Set #Temp, #KantoReg\par
Else\par
If #CSRegn = 2\par
/Set #Temp, #JohtoReg\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, #HoennReg\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:ChampMems\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21)) & " = " & $GetValue("TPos_" & $Mid($GetValue($Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21) & "_ChampionShip"), 4, 1)) & " in Tier " & $Mid($Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21) & "_ChampionShip"), 5, 1) & "."\par
If #TempB < #Temp\par
GoTo ChampMems\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Championship has not begun yet!"\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "CSStats"\par
If #CSRegn > 0\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE($GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship's current status") & " ***"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The registered members of the " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#CSRegn)) & " Chamionship are:" \par
:CSStats\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Participants in Tier " & $Str(#Temp) & " are:"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp)\f0 )\par
/Set #TempA, $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Mems"\f0 )\par
/Set #TempB, $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Max"\f0 )\par
/Set #TempC, $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Match"\f0 )\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Round"\f0 )\par
If $TempA = "X"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Participants in Tier " & $Str(#Temp) & " have all been disqualified."\par
Else\par
If $TempA = "A" OR $TempA = "B"\par
/Set #TempD, #GetValue("\f1 ChampBracket_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Match_1"\f0 )\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp, (#TempD * 21) + (#TempD - 21), 21)\par
/SendPM #Source, "1: " & \f1 $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & " is currently in the " & $GetValue("TPos_" & $Mid($GetValue($TempB & "_Championship"), 4, 1)) & "."\f0\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Participants in Tier " & $Str(#Temp) & " are in the Preliminary Round " & $TempA & "."\par
\f1 /Set #SendCS, 1\par
\f0 /Set #TempB, #Temp\par
GoTo CSBracket\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
:StatsReturn\par
If #Temp < 4\par
GoTo CSStats\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Championship has not begun yet!"\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 4) = "Join"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Badges")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:JoinRegion\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 4) & " Region" = $GetValue("Region_" & $Str(#Temp))\par
/Set #TempA, #GetValue("ChampionShip_" & $Str(#Temp))\par
If #TempA = #Val($Mid($Temp,14 ,3))\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/Set #TempC, #KantoReg\par
Else\par
If #Temp = 2\par
/Set #TempC, #JohtoReg\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, #HoennReg\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("ChampionShip_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Registrants"), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID)) = 0\par
If #TempC < 32\par
If $Mid($TempA, (#Temp*8) + (#Temp-8), 8) = "11111111"\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, (#Temp*8) + (#Temp-8) - 1) & "00000000" & $Right($TempA, #Len($TempA) - #Val((#Temp*8) + (#Temp-8) + 7))\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Badges", $TempA\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": To register your badges will be taken!"\par
/SaveValue "ChampionShip_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Registrants", $GetValue("ChampionShip_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Registrants") & $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & ","\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " has just registered for the " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship!"\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/Inc #KantoReg\par
/Set #TempD, #KantoReg\par
Else\par
If #Temp = 2\par
/Inc #JohtoReg\par
/Set #TempD, #JohtoReg\par
Else\par
/Inc #HoennReg\par
/Set #TempD, #HoennReg\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($Temp, 11) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp, 12, 2)) - 8), 2) & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - 13)\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You don't have all 8 badges for this region to register!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The registration has been closed!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have already registered!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The registration is not here!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #Temp < 3\par
GoTo JoinRegion\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": That is not even a championship to join!"\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "Import"\par
If $Str(#Val($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Tokens"))) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You don't have any Tokens to Import!"\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": How many of your " & $Str(#Val($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Tokens"))) & " Tokens, do you want to sell? (Each token is worth $200)"\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#Val($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Tokens"))) \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 73\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "Watch"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Current RPG Time is " & $Str(#DayT) & ":00 " & $GetValue("Day_" & $Str(#Day)) & "."\par
If #Day = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotname & ": The Sun is up and it is currently day time."\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotname & ": The Moon is bright showing no sign of daylight."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "Reset"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 6\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Are you sure you want to delete your team. Type !Yes or !No to answer."\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 7) = "Donate "\par
/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 7)) \par
If #Temp = 0 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 7) & " trainer is still asleep somewhere!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
If $Right($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_RPGStats"),1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " has their RPG Mode OFF!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
If $Left($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_RPGStats"),1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " has not yet initialized their team!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": How much do you want to donate to " & $Name(#Temp) & "?"\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID)\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 83\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "Showteam"\par
:ShowTeam\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is...."\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:ShowTPoke\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45),45)\par
/Set $TempB, $Right($TempA, 18)\par
If $Left($TempA, 3) <> "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Pokemon" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,4,3))) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "Stats: It needs " & $Str(#Val($Left($TempB, 6))) & " experience points to grow to Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,4,3)) + 1) & "."\par
If $Right($TempB, 3) <> "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Evos: Its trying to evolve into " & $Pokemon(#Val($Right($TempB, 3))) & ". Type !Pokemon to find out how to evolve it."\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($TempB, 7, 9) <> "000000000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Moves: Its trying to learn new moves. Type !Pokemon to find out how to teach them."\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "Item: " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Mid($TempA, 7, 1) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 8, 2)))) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "Move1: " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempA, 10, 3))) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "Move2: " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempA, 13, 3))) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "Move3: " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempA, 16, 3))) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "Move4: " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempA, 19, 3))) & "."\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesOT")\par
/Set #TempC, #IsIn($TempC,"*" & $Str(#Temp - 1))\par
/Set #TempD, #IsIn($TempC,"*" & $Str(#Temp))\par
/SendPM #Source, "OriginalTrainer(OT): " & $Mid($TempC, #TempC + 2, #TempD - (#TempC + 2)) & "."\par
/SendPM #Source, "TrainerID: " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 22, 6))) & "."\par
If #Temp < 6 AND #Val($Mid($Temp, ((#Temp+1)*45)+((#Temp+1)-45), 3)) > 0\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
GoTo ShowTPoke\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 2\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Cmd, 9) = "Showteam "\par
/Set #Temp, #PNumber($Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 9)) \par
If #Temp = 0 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Cmd, #Len($Cmd) - 9) & " trainer is still asleep somewhere!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
If $Right($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_RPGStats"),1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " has their RPG Mode OFF!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
If $Left($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_RPGStats"),1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & " has not yet initialized their team!"\par
/Exit \par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "" \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Temp) & "'s team:"\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:ShowTeamOne\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempA*45)+(#TempA-45),45)\par
If $Left($TempA, 3) <> "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Pokemon " & $Str(#TempA) & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " at Lv " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,4,3))) & " with the item " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Mid($TempA, 7, 1) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 8, 2)))) & "."\par
If #TempA < 6\par
GoTo ShowTeamOne\par
Else\par
/Inc #TempA\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 17\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#TempA)\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#TempA) & ": Cancel."\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "" \par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "TeamCheck"\par
/Set #Team(#Source), 0\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 0\par
:TeamChecker\par
If $Right($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes"),45) = "000000000000000000000000000000000000000000000"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized but not full yet so you can't battle."\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized and full so your team will now be validated."\par
/Set #Team(#Source), 1\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
If #Temp < 6\par
GoTo PokeChecker\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:PokeChecker\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #GetTeamPoke(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " in position " & $Str(#Temp) & " in our records. You don't have it in your team, the wrong Pok\'e9mon is " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#Source,#Temp)) & "."\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #GetPokeLevel(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 3,3))\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " is not at Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 3,3))) & "!" \par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6,3)) > 412 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6,3)) < 475\par
If #GetPokeItem(#Source, #Temp) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 7,2)) \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " does not have the item " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 6, 1) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 7,2)))) & " with it!" \par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #GetPokeItem(#Source, #Temp) <> 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " does not have the item (No Item) with it!" \par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:MoveChecker\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If #HasPokeMove(#Source, #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3)), #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempA * 2) + (#TempA - 2),3)) ) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid! Please make sure our records match your team. Or your not allowed to battle!"\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:MoveChecks\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
:MoveChecking\par
/Inc #TempC\par
If #GetPokeMove(#Source,#Temp,#TempB) <> #Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempC * 2) + (#TempC - 2),3)) \par
If #TempC < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecking\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45),3))) & " has the move " & $Move(#Val($Mid($Temp,(#Temp * 45) + (#Temp - 45) + 8 + (#TempA * 2) + (#TempA - 2),3))) & " in our record. You don't have it in your team, the wrong move is " & $Move(#GetPokeMove(#Source,#Temp,#TempB)) & "."\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 100\par
GoTo RPGON\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #TempB < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecks\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #TempA < 4\par
GoTo MoveChecker\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 6\par
GoTo PokeChecker\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Valid(#Source), 1 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is initialized, full and valid so you can battle now."\par

EndIf\par
If #IsIn($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Seen_Poke"), "," & "080" & ",") = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Seen_Poke")\par

/Set $TempB, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($TempB,20) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempB, 21, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 23)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:SlowEvo\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45),45)\par
If #Val($Left($TempA, 3)) = 79 AND #Val($Mid($TempA, 7, 3)) <> 113 AND #Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) > 36\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Left($Temp, (#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45) - 1) & "080" & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#Temp*45)+(#Temp-45) + 2))\par
GoTo SpecialCmd \par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 6 \par
GoTo SlowEvo\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Darn! Its just another Magikarp, there it goes.."\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You don't have a slowpoke that wants to evolve."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par

Else\par

GoTo FlyMsg\par
EndIf\par

/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#TempC)\par
Else\par

\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " has just passed the " & \f0 $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & ", Congratulations!"\par
\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": Now " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " faces the infamous Elite 4!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
\f0 /SaveValue $TempA & "_ChampionShip", $Left($GetValue($TempA & "_ChampionShip"), 3) & "4" & $Mid($GetValue($TempA & "_ChampionShip"), 5, 1) & "01"\f1\par
\f0 /SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round", "A"\par
\f1 /Exit\par
Else\par
\f0 /SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round", \f1 #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round"\f1 )) + 1\f0\par
\f1 /SendAll ""\par
\f0 /SendAll "*** " & $UCASE($GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round Announcement") & " ***"\par
\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": The " & \f0 $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & " \f1 has just entered Round " & $Str(#Tourney-1) & "!"\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": There are " & $GetValue(\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Mem"\f1 ) & " members who are still in the \f0 Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & " \f1 out of " & $GetValue(\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Max"\f1 ) & " players!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:CSVal\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right("0" & $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)), 2) & ","\par
If #Temp < #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo CSVal\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:DelCS\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), ""\par
If #TempA < 8\par
GoTo DelCS\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, \f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))\f1\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": Randomizing \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Brackets......."\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:RandomCS\par
/Set #TempC, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($TempC,(#TempC*2) + (#TempC-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempA & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set #TempC, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempC,(#TempC*2) + (#TempC-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempB & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempA)*21) + (#Val($TempA)-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), $TempB & "-" & $TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match", #TempA\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue($TempD & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempD & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue($TempE & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempE & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
If #Temp > 1\par
GoTo RandomCS\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": A random player is given a Bye to the next round because of the lack of an opponent!"\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($TempC,2)\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Left($TempC,2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempC*21) + (#TempC-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($TempA & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempA & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempB, 3) & "2" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2) \par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match", #TempA\par
EndIf\par
/Set #SendCS, 0\par
GoTo CSBracket\par
:CSBracket\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Bracket listings are as follows."\par
Else\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Bracket listings are as follows..."\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, \f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))\f1\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:CSMatchShow\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)), "-") > 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Right($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21)+(#TempA-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp,(#TempC*21)+(#TempC-21),21)\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)\par
EndIf\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)) = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)\par
EndIf\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)))\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21)) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))\par
EndIf\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
GoTo CSMatchShow\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB < 4\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
GoTo StatsReturn\par
Else\par
GoTo \f0 OBOReturn\f1\par
\f0 EndIf\par
EndIf\f1\par
If #SendCS = 0\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\f0\par
:WildLose\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
If #Cash(#Source) <> 0 \par
/Set #Temp, #Int(#Cash(#Source)/20)\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats", $Left($Temp,2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Health(#Source) - #Rand(5,2)),3) & $Right("00000" & $Str(#Val(#Cash(#Source)) - #Val(#Temp)),6) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - 11)\par
Else\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You lost $" & $Str(#Temp) & " for losing!"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempD, 0\par
:LosePoke\par
/Inc #TempD\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempD*45) + (#TempD-45),45)\par
If $Left($TempA,6) <> $Left($TeamPoke(#Source),6) AND $Mid($TempA,10,12) <> $Mid($TeamPoke(#Source),7,12)\par
If #TempD < 6\par
GoTo LosePoke\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source), 3))\par
If #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Love_0") > 0 OR #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Love_1") > 0 OR #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Love_2") > 0 \par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesLove")\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($TempC,(#TempD*7) + (#TempD-7),7)\par
/Set #TempI, #Val($Right($TempD, 2))\par
/Set #TempJ, #Val($Left($TempD, 1))\par
/Set #TempK, #Val($Mid($TempD, 2, 2))\par
/Set #TempL, #Val($Mid($TempD, 4, 2))\par
If #TempD = 1\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI + 1\par
EndIf\par
If #TempK = 8\par
/Set #TempJ, #TempJ + 1\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI - 4\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI - 2\par
/Set #TempJ, 1\par
/Set #TempK, 8\par
EndIf\par
If #TempI > 20\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI - 20 + #TempL\par
EndIf\par
If #TempJ > 9 \par
/Set #TempJ, 9\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempD, $Str(#TempJ) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempK), 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempL), 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempI), 2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Left($TempC, (#TempD*7) + (#TempD-7) - 1) & $TempD & $Right($TempC, #Len($TempC) - (#Val(#TempD * 7) + #Val(#TempD - 7) + 6))\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesLove", $TempC\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
/Set #Quite(#Source), 5\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
/Exit\par
:Exp\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
/Set #TempF, #Val($Mid($WildPoke(#Source),4,3))\par
/Set #TempE, #Val($Mid($TeamPoke(#Source),4,3))\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempM, 0\par
:ExpPoke\par
/Inc #TempM\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempM*45) + (#TempM-45),45)\par
/Set $TempB, $Right($TempA, 18)\par
If $Left($TempA,6) <> $Left($TeamPoke(#Source),6) AND $Mid($TempA,10,12) <> $Mid($TeamPoke(#Source),7,12)\par
If #TempD < 6\par
GoTo ExpPoke\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, #Val((#TempM* 45) + (#TempM- 45))\par
/Set #TempB, #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 1) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 2) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 3) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 4) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 5) + #GetPokeLevel(#Source, 6)\par
/Set #TempC, #TempF * 6\par
/Set #TempD, #TempE\par
/Set #TempE, #TempF\par
/Set #TempF, #GetValue("Exp_" & $GetValue("P_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_E") & "_Lv_" & $Str(#TempD))\par
/Set #TempG, #GetValue("Exp_" & $GetValue("P_" & $Str(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))) & "_E") & "_Lv_" & $Str(#TempE))\par
/Set #TempH, #Round(#Round(((#TempF/#TempD)*(#TempG/#TempE)) / (#TempF/#TempC)) * .4)\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & " gained " & $Str(#TempH) & " experience points."\par
If #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_0") > 0 OR #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_1") > 0 OR #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_2") > 0 \par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesLove")\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($TempC,(#TempM*7) + (#TempM-7),7)\par
/Set #TempI, #Val($Right($TempD, 2))\par
/Set #TempJ, #Val($Left($TempD, 1))\par
/Set #TempK, #Val($Mid($TempD, 2, 2))\par
/Set #TempL, #Val($Mid($TempD, 4, 2))\par
If #TempM= 1\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI + 1\par
EndIf\par
If #TempK = 2\par
/Set #TempJ, #TempJ + 1\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI  + 1\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI + 2\par
/Set #TempJ, 1\par
/Set #TempK, 2\par
EndIf\par
If #TempJ > 9 \par
/Set #TempJ, 9\par
EndIf\par
If #TempH >= #Val($Left($TempB, 6)) \par
/Set #TempI, #TempI + 4\par
/Set #TempJ, 1\par
/Set #TempK, 5\par
EndIf\par
If #TempI > 20\par
/Set #TempI, #TempI - 20 + #TempL\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempD, $Str(#TempJ) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempK), 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempL), 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempI), 2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Left($TempC, (#TempM*7) + (#TempM-7) - 1) & $TempD & $Right($TempC, #Len($TempC) - (#Val(#TempM* 7) + #Val(#TempM- 7) + 6))\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesLove", $TempC\par
EndIf\par
:LevelGrow\par
If #TempH >= #Val($Left($TempB, 6)) \par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " just grew to level " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) + 1) & "!"\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, 3) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) + 1), 3) & $Right($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 6)\par
/Set #TempH, #TempH - #Val($Left($TempB, 6))\par
/Set $TempB, $Right("00000" & $Str(#GetValue("Exp_" & $Str(#GetValue("P_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_E")) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) + 1)) - (#TempH - #Val($Left($TempB, 6)))), 6) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - 6)\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_by_1") <> ""\par
If #Val($Left($TempA, 3)) = 79\par
If #Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) = 37\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your Slowpoke now has the urge to fish with its tail!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Left($TempA, 3)) = 290\par
If #Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) = 20\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(291) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & "291"\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Left($TempA, 3)) = 265\par
If #Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) = 7\par
If #DayT < 9 AND #Day = 2 OR #DayT > 7 AND #Day = 1\par
/Set #TempI, 266\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, 268\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#TempI) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Str(#TempI)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Left($TempA, 3)) = 236\par
If #Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) = 20\par
If #DayT > 9 AND #Day = 1 OR #DayT < 6 AND #Day = 2\par
/Set #TempI, 106\par
Else\par
If #DayT > 5 AND #Day = 2 OR #DayT < 2 AND #Day = 1\par
/Set #TempI, 107\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, 237\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#TempI) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Str(#TempI)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_PokesLove")\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($TempC,(#TempM*7) + (#TempM-7),7)\par
If #Val($Right($TempD, 2)) > 18\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_0") > 0 OR $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_1") > 0 OR $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_2") > 0 \par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_1") > 0\par
If #DayT > 5 AND #Day = 2 OR #DayT < 2 AND #Day = 1\par
GoTo NotLoveEvo\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempI, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_1")\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_2") > 0\par
If #DayT > 9 AND #Day = 1 OR #DayT < 6 AND #Day = 2\par
GoTo NotLoveEvo\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempI, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_2")\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & "_Love_0")\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#TempI) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempI), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
:NotLoveEvo\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to learn the move " & $Move(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3))))) & "!"\par
/Set #TempI, 7\par
:PokeEvoMove\par
If #TempI < 14\par
If $Mid($TempB,#TempI,3) <> "000"\par
/Inc #TempI, + 3\par
GoTo PokeEvoMove\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempI, 7\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB, #TempI - 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3))))), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - (#TempI + 2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To") <> ""\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "!"\par
Else\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To") <> ""\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To"), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $Getplayerinfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo LevelGrow\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $Right("00000" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempB, 6)) - #TempH), 6) & $Right($TempB, #Len($TempB) - 6)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, #TempA - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TempA + 44))\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " needs " & $Str(#Val($Left($TempB,6))) & " experience points to grow to Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) + 1) & "!"\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Quite(#Source), 5\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
/Exit\par
:Battle\par
If #WildSt(#Source) = 6 OR #WildSt(#Source) = 5 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))) & " is hurt by " & $GetValue("Status_" & $Str(#WildSt(#Source)) & "_Half") & "!"\par
/Set #WildPoke(#Source), #WildPoke(#Source) - 2\par
If #WildPoke(#Source) < 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))) & " fainted!"\par
GoTo Exp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #TeamSt(#Source) = 6 Or #TeamSt(#Source) = 5\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & " is hurt by " & $GetValue("Status_" & $Str(#TeamSt(#Source)) & "_Half") & "!"\par
/Set #TeamPoke(#Source), #TeamPoke(#Source) - 2\par
If #TeamPoke(#Source) < 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & " fainted!"\par
GoTo WildLose\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your battle continues ..."\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
/SendPM #Source, "                                                              " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))) & " Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($WildPoke(#Source),4,3))) & " [ " & $GetValue("Status_" & $Str(#WildSt(#Source))) & " ]"\par
/Set $TempB, ""\par
/Set #Temp, #Int(#WildPoke(#Source) / 5)\par
:WildHealth\par
If #Temp <> 0 \par
/Inc #Temp, - 1\par
/Set $TempB, $TempB & "\'9a"\par
GoTo WildHealth\par
EndIf\par
If #Len($TempB) < 20\par
/Set $TempB, $TempB & " "\par
GoTo WildHealth\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "                                                                 ___________"\par
/SendPM #Source, "                                                                 |" & $TempB & "|   " & $Str(#WildPoke(#Source)) & "%"\par
/SendPM #Source, "                                                                 \'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af"\par
If $GetValue("PokeSprite_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempD, $GetValue("PokeSprite_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))))\par
/Set $TempD, $Replace($TempD, "[]", $Chr(13))\par
/SendPM #Source, $TempD\par
/Set $TempD, $GetValue("PokeSprite2_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($WildPoke(#Source),3))))\par
/Set $TempD, $Replace($TempD, "[]", $Chr(13))\par
/SendPM #Source, $TempD\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))) & " Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TeamPoke(#Source),4,3))) & " [ " & $GetValue("Status_" & $Str(#TeamSt(#Source))) & " ]"\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #TempA, #Int(#TeamPoke(#Source) / 5)\par
:TeamHealth\par
If #TempA <> 0 \par
/Inc #TempA, - 1\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & "\'9a"\par
GoTo TeamHealth\par
EndIf\par
If #Len($TempC) < 20\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & " "\par
GoTo TeamHealth\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "___________"\par
/SendPM #Source, "|" & $TempC & "|   " & $Str(#TeamPoke(#Source)) & "%"\par
/SendPM #Source, "\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af\'af"\par
If $GetValue("PokeSpriteBack_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempD, $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) &  $Chr(9) & $GetValue("PokeSpriteBack_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))))\par
/Set $TempD, $Replace($TempD, "[]", $Chr(13) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) &  $Chr(9))\par
/SendPM #Source, $TempD\par
/Set $TempD, $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) &  $Chr(9) & $GetValue("PokeSpriteBack2_" &  $Str(#Val($Left($TeamPoke(#Source),3))))\par
/Set $TempD, $Replace($TempD, "[]", $Chr(13) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) & $Chr(9) &  $Chr(9))\par
/SendPM #Source, $TempD\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": What do you want to do?"\par
/SendPM #Source, "1: Attack - to use an attack on the Wild Pok\'e9mon."\par
/SendPM #Source, "2: Catch - to try and catch it with a Pok\'e9ball."\par
/SendPM #Source, "3: Throw - to throw something at it(some food or a rock)."\par
/SendPM #Source, "4: Flute - to use Pok\'e9flute on it."\par
/SendPM #Source, "5: Run - to try and escape."\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 52\par
/Exit\par
:SpecialCmd\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), "000000000000000000000"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_Pokes")\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
:SpcCmdPoke\par
/Inc #TempB\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45),3)) = 79 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 6,3)) <> 113 AND #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 3,3)) > 36\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),20) & "1"\par
EndIf\par
:SpcCmdMove\par
/Inc #TempC\par
/Set #TempD, #Val($Mid($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 8 + (#TempC * 2) + (#TempC - 2),3))\par
If #TempD = 39\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),20)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 217\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),1) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),19)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 245\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),2) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),18)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 246\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),3) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),17)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 168\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),4) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),16)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 208\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),5) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),15)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 71\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),6) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),14)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 271\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),7) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),13)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 43\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),13) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),7)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 227\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),14) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),6)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 72\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),15) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),5)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempD = 88\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),16) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),4)\par
EndIf\par
If #TempC < 4\par
GoTo SpcCmdMove\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB < 6\par
GoTo SpcCmdPoke\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:SpecIts\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2) <> "00"\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) > 1 AND #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) < 7\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) \par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),#TempA + 6) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source), 20 - (#TempA + 6))\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemk"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 58\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),17) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),3)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2) <> "00"\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 11\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),18) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),2)\par
EndIf\par
If #Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_itemi"),(#Temp*3)+(#Temp-3),2)) = 84\par
/Set $SpcCmd(#Source), $Left($SpcCmd(#Source),19) & "1" & $Right($SpcCmd(#Source),1)\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo SpecIts\par
EndIf\par
If $Cmd = "Rope" OR $Str(#Phase(#Source)) = "82"\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 82\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0\par
EndIf\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:Winner\par
If $Sign(#TempA) <> $Str(#TempD)\par
/Set #TempE, #TempA\par
/Set #TempA, #Temp\par
/Set #Temp, #TempE\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": Congratulations! You won the game!"\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": You lost! Sorry but " & $Name(#TempA) & " won it!"\par
/SendAll $GameBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempA) & " has beaten " & $Name(#Temp) & " in a TicTacToe game!"\par
/SendPM #TempA, $BotName & ": You earned 2 Tokens!"\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_Tokens", #GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_Tokens") + 2 \par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_are") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_are") \par
If $Mid($Temp,29,2) = "99"\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp,28) & "01" & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - 30)\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": Your Losing score has reached the maximum. It will be reset!"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp,28) & $Right("0" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,29,2)) + 1),2) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - 30)\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($TempA,27,2) = "99"\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA,PSID) & "_are", $Left($TempA,26) & "01" & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - 28)\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": Your Winning score has reached the maximum. It will be reset!"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA,PSID) & "_are", $Left($TempA,26) & $Right("0" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,27,2)) + 1),2) & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - 28)\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Temp), 0\par
/Set #Phase(#TempA), 0\par
/Set $TicTacToe(#Temp), ""\par
/Set $TicTacToe(#TempA), ""\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("Server_Data_Game_Champs_is")\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("Server_Data_Game_Len")\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Mid($GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_are"),27,2))\par
If #TempC >= #Val($Mid($TempA,#Val($Left($TempB, 2)) + 3, 2))\par
/SaveValue "Server_Data_Game_Champs_is", $Name(#TempA) & " " & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempC), 2) & $Right($TempA, #Len($TempA) - (#Val($Left($TempB,2)) + 3))\par
/SaveValue "Server_Data_Game_Len", $Right("00" & $Str(#Len($Name(#TempA))), 2) & $Right($TempB, 6)\par
/SendAll $GameBotName & ": Attention! " & $Name(#TempA) & " has just beaten the highest TicTacToe wins record on the server! " & $Name(#TempA) & " just became this servers TicTacToe Champion, His/Her Wins are " & $Str(#TempC) & ". Congratulate them!"\par
/SendPM #TempA, $BotName & ": You earned 10 Tokens!"\par
/SaveValue $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_Tokens", #GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_Tokens") + 10\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:TicTacToe\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": Your games progress is ...."\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": Your games progress is ...."\par
/Set #TempB, 1\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
/SendPM #Temp, "-----A-------B-------C----"\par
/SendPM #TempA, "-----A-------B-------C----"\par
:TTT\par
/SendPM #Temp, "[" & $Str(#TempC) & "]  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB,1)) & "  I  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB + 1,1)) & "  I  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB + 2,1))\par
/SendPM #TempA, "[" & $Str(#TempC) & "]  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB,1)) & "  I  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB + 1,1)) & "  I  " & $GetValue("Sign_" & $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),#TempB + 2,1))\par
If #TempB < 7\par
/SendPM #Temp, "---------------------------"\par
/SendPM #TempA, "---------------------------"\par
/Inc #TempB, + 3\par
/Inc #TempC\par
GoTo TTT\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempD, 0\par
:TTTPNum\par
/Inc #TempD\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),1,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),2,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),3,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),4,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),5,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),6,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),7,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),8,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),9,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),1,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),4,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),7,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),2,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),5,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),8,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),3,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),6,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),9,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),1,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),5,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),9,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),3,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),5,1) = $Str(#TempD) AND $Mid($TicTacToe(#Temp),7,1) = $Str(#TempD)\par
GoTo Winner\par
Else\par
If #TempD < 2\par
GoTo TTTPNum\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #IsIn($TicTacToe(#Temp),"0") = 0\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": Your game has tied!"\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": Your game has tied!"\par
/SendAll $GameBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempA) & " has tied with " & $Name(#Temp) & " in a TicTacToe game!"\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, PSID) & "_are") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA, PSID) & "_are") \par
If $Mid($Temp,31,2) = "99"\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp,30) & "01" & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - 32)\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": Your Tieing score has reached the maximum. It will be reset!"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp,PSID) & "_are", $Left($Temp,30) & $Right("0" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,31,2)) + 1),2) & $Right($Temp,#Len($Temp) - 32)\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($TempA,31,2) = "99"\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA,PSID) & "_are", $Left($TempA,30) & "01" & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - 32)\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": Your Tieing score has reached the maximum. It will be reset!"\par
Else\par
/SaveValue "The_Stats_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempA,PSID) & "_are", $Left($TempA,30) & $Right("0" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA,31,2)) + 1),2) & $Right($TempA,#Len($TempA) - 32)\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Phase(#Temp), 0\par
/Set #Phase(#TempA), 0\par
/Set $TicTacToe(#Temp), ""\par
/Set $TicTacToe(#TempA), ""\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Temp, $GameBotName & ": It is " & $Name(#TempA) & "'s turn now!"\par
/SendPM #TempA, $GameBotName & ": It is your turn now! Type the grid number like 'A1' or 'C3'!"\par
/Exit\par
:OBOItem\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Right($Area(#Source),4) & "'s " & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source)) & " Items:"\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Str(#Len($GetValue($Right($Area(#Source),4) & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3))) & "_Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"))) / 2)\par
/Set #Temp, 0 \par
/Set #TempA, 0 \par
:OneByOneItems\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($GetValue($Right($Area(#Source),4) & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3))) & "_Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Temp,2) <> "" \par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp + #TempA) & ": " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($Right($Area(#Source),4) & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3))) & "_Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Temp,2)))) & " = $" & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($Right($Area(#Source),4) & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp,14,3))) & "_Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short")),#Temp,2))) & "_Price") & "."\par
If #Temp + #TempA < #Val($EditInfo(#Source))\par
/Inc #TempA, -1\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo OneByOneItems\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:OBOItemBox\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & "'s " & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source)) & " " & $ExtraInfo(#Source) & "s:"\par
/Set $Temp, $ExtraInfo(#Source)\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 78\par
/Set $ExtraInfo(#Source), $EditInfo(#Source)\par
EndIf\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_" & $Temp & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short"))\par
/Set #Temp, 0 \par
:OneByOneBoxItems\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $Mid($EditInfo(#Source),(#Temp*3) + (#Temp-3),2) <> "00" \par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $ExtrInfo(#Source) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($EditInfo(#Source),(#Temp*3) + (#Temp-3),2)))) & " = " & $Str(#Val($Mid($EditInfo(#Source),(#Temp*3) + (#Temp-3) + 2,2))) & "."\par
If #Temp < 10\par
GoTo OneByOneBoxItems\par
EndIf\par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Str(#Temp)\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": (No Item)." \par
/Set $EditInfo(#Source), $Str(#Temp-1)\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:ItemBox\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:ItemTypeBox\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/SendPM #Source, $Name(#Source) & "'s " & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " BoxItems:"\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:ItemSlotBox\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Short")),(#TempA*3)+(#TempA-3),2) = "00"\par
/SendPM #Source, "Slot " & $Str(#TempA) & ": None."\par
If #Temp < 4\par
GoTo ItemTypeBox\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, "Slot " & $Str(#TempA) & ": " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Short")),(#TempA*3)+(#TempA-3),2)))) & " = " & $Mid($GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_BoxItem" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Str(#Temp) & "_Short")),(#TempA*3)+(#TempA-3) + 2,2) & "."\par
If #TempA < 10\par
GoTo ItemSlotBox\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < 4\par
GoTo ItemTypeBox\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If $ExtrInfo(#Source) = "1"\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), ""\par
GoTo ItemComp\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:ShowDatabase\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Your Pok\'e9mon boxes:"\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:Data\par
/Inc #Temp\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#Temp) & "Pokes")\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:Database\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempA * 45) + (#TempA - 45), 45)\par
If $Left($TempA, 3) <> "000"\par
If #TempA < 20\par
GoTo Database\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": Pok\'e9monBox is FULL [20/20] Pok\'e9mon stored."\par
If #Temp < 5\par
GoTo Data\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#Temp) & ": Pok\'e9monBox has [" & $Str(#TempA - 1) & "/20] Pok\'e9mon stored."\par
If #Temp < 5\par
GoTo Data\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Source, "6: Exit."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:ShowBox\par

/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetplayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_Box" & $Str(#Temp) & "Pokes")\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:BoxLoop\par

/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempA * 45) + (#TempA - 45), 45)\par
If $Left($TempA, 3) <> "000"\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#TempA) & ": " & $Pokemon($Left($TempA,3)) & " at Lv " & $Str($Mid($TempA,4,3)) & " with " & $GetValue("Item_" & $GetValue("Item_Type_" & $Mid($TempA, 7, 1) & "_Short") & "_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 8, 2)))) & "."\par
If #TempA < 20\par
GoTo BoxLoop\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #TempA\par
Else\par
If #TempA = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: The Pok\'e9monBox is empty!"\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 18\par
/SendPM #Source, "Computer: Withdrawal cancelled!"\par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 14\par

EndIf\par

EndIf\par
If $ExtrInfo(#Source) = "1"\par
GoTo PokeComp\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $Str(#TempA) & ": Exit."\par
/Set $ExtrInfo(#Source), $Str(#TempA)\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:NewInfo\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par
/Set #Cash(#Source), #Val($Mid($TempA, 6, 6))\par
/Set #Health(#Source), #Val($Mid($TempA, 3, 3))\par
/Set $Area(#Source), $GetValue("Area_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 14, 3))))\par
:NewInfoIn\par

If $Name(#Source) = "Mew Master" OR $Name(#Source) = "Lord Meshadieme" OR $Name(#Source) = "Lamel"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Source, EXTR, "[Creator of this RPG - " & $Extrinfo(#Source)  \par
Else \par
If $Name(#Source) = "Bikaben"\par

Else\par

EndIf \par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Source), $GetPlayerInfo(#Source, EXTR)\par
If #Phase(#Source) = 51 OR #Phase(#Source) = 61 OR #Phase(#Source) = 55 OR #Phase(#Source) = 73 OR #Phase(#Source) = 33 OR #Phase(#Source) = 80 OR #Phase(#Source) = 49 OR #Phase(#Source) = 60 OR #Phase(#Source) = 83 \par
If #Phase(#Source) = 73 OR #Phase(#Source) = 80 OR #Phase(#Source) = 49 OR #Phase(#Source) = 60 OR #Phase(#Source) = 83 \par
/Set #Phase(#Source), 0 \par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source, PSID) & "_RPGStats") \par

/Exit\par

:RoundCheck\par
If #Tourney = 1\par

/Exit\par

:RandomMatch\par

/Set $TempA, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempA & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempB & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempA)*21) + (#Val($TempA)-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par

/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempE, $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par

GoTo RandomMatch\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A random player is given a Bye to the next round because of the lack of an opponent!"\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($TempC,2)\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Left($TempC,2))\par

/Set #Send, 0\par

:ShowBracket\par
If #Send = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": Match bracket listings are as follows."\par
Else\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Match bracket listings are as follows..."\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:TourneyMatchShow\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)), "-") > 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Right($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21)+(#TempA-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21)\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)\par
EndIf\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)) = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)\par
EndIf\par
If #Send = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)))\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21)) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))\par
EndIf\par
If #Send = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
GoTo TourneyMatchShow\par
EndIf\par
If #Send = 0\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
:NotSkip\par
EndEvent\par

:MonoSpec\par

/Set #TempG, 1\par
:MonoSpecies\par
/Inc #TempG\par
If #GetTeamPoke(#TempE,#TempG) = #TempF\par
If #TempG < 6\par
GoTo MonoSpecies\par
Else\par
If #TempE = #Source\par
/Set #TempE, #Target\par
GoTo MonoSpec\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempE) & "'s team is not a MonoSpecies Team."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #TourneyType = 30 OR #TourneyType = 28 OR #TourneyType = 27 OR #TourneyType = 3 OR #TourneyType = 4 OR #TourneyType = 5 OR #TourneyType = 6 OR #TourneyType = 7 OR #TourneyType = 8 OR #TourneyType = 10 OR #TourneyType = 12 OR #TourneyType = 14 OR #TourneyType = 15\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType) & "_Short"))\par
/Set #TempC, 1\par
If #TourneyType = 4 \par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right($GetValue("UE"), #Len($GetValue("UE")) - 1)\par

/Set #TempC, 5\par

/Set #TempC, 4\par

/Set #TempE, 1\par
/Set #TempF, 0\par
/Set #TempG, 0\par
:TourTier\par

/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempD) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#TempD, #TempE)) & " is not at Level 5!"\par

/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #IsIn($TempC, $Chr(44) & $Str(#GetTeamPoke(#TempD, #TempE)) & $Chr(44)) = 0\par
If #TourneyType = 4 OR #TourneyType = 6\par
If #TourneyType = 4\par
/Set $TempD, $GetValue("UU")\par
Else\par
/Set $TempD, $GetValue("BL")\par

EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Inc #TempF\par

/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempD) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#GetTeamPoke(#TempD, #TempE)) & " is not a Valid " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Pok\'e9mon!"\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
:SecTier\par
If #TempE < 6 \par
/Inc #TempE\par
GoTo TourTier\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempD, #Target\par
/Set #TempE, 1\par
/Set #TempF, 0\par
GoTo TourTier\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempD, 0\par

/Set $Temp, $Temp & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempD), 2)\par

/Set #TempG, 1\par

If #TempG < 6\par
/Inc #TempG\par
GoTo MonoT\par

If #TempE + 1 < #TempD\par
/Inc #TempE, +2\par
GoTo MonoType\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": " & $Name(#TempC) & "'s team is not a MonoType Team."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par

/Set #TempC, #Target\par
/Set #TempD, 0\par

/Set #TempD, 0\par

:MColor\par

/Set $Temp, $Temp & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempD), 2)\par

/Set #TempE, 1\par

/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #TempE < 6 \par
/Inc #TempE\par
GoTo MetroItem\par

/Set #TempF, #Target\par
/Set #TempE, 1\par
GoTo MetroItem\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp, 4, 1)) = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": Your Tournament match is waiting. Use !Commands to view your other options."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Source\par
/Set #TempA, #Target\par
/Set #TempF, #Temp\par
/Set #TempC, 0\par
/Set #TempD, 0\par

/Set #TempE, 1\par
:Cheaper\par
If $Mid($Temp,#TempE,1) = "1"\par

/Inc #TempC\par
Else\par
/Inc #TempD\par

If #IsIn($TempE, "," & $Str(#GetTeamPoke(#TempB, #TempE)) & ",") > 0\par

/Inc #TempC\par

/SendPM #Temp, $BotName & ": You have Ubers and your Uber Status off."\par

If #Val($TempH) > 0\par
/Set $TempE, $Left($GetValue("The_BattleRules_of_" & $GetPlayerInfo(#TempC, PSID) & "_are"), 12)\par
/Set #TempD, 1\par
/Set #TempE, 0\par
:ChallengeCheck\par
If $Mid($TempE, #TempD, 1) <> $Mid($Message, #TempD, 1)\par

/SendPM #TempC, $BotName & ": " & $Name(#TempB) & "'s Challenge violate's the " & $GetValue("ChalCntrl_" & $Str(#TempD)) & " Challenge Control."\par

/Inc #TempE\par

/Inc #TempD\par
GoTo ChallengeCheck\par

:PokeMoveCheck\par

If #HasPoke(#TempB, #Val($Mid($TempF, #TempD, 3))) = 1 \par
If $TempD = "1"\par
/SendPM #TempC, $BotName & ": " & $Name(#TempB) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($TempF, #TempD, 3))) & " violates your controls."\par

/Inc #TempE\par

If $TempD = "1"\par
/SendPM #TempC, $BotName & ": " & $Name(#TempB) & "'s " & $Pokemon(#Val($Mid($TempG, #TempF, 3))) & " with " & $Move(#Val($Mid($TempG, #TempF + 3, 3))) & " violates your controls."\par

/Inc #TempE\par
