/Inc #TempF, 6\par
/Inc #TempD, 3\par
If #TempF < #Len($TempG) OR #TempD < #Len($TempF)\par
Goto PokeMoveCheck\par
Else\par
If #Val($TempD) = 2 AND #TempE > #Val($Right($GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#TempB) & "_is"), 1))\par
If #TempB = #Source\par
/SendPM #TempB, $BotName & ": Your challenge violates " & $Str(#TempE) & " out of " & $Str(#Val($Right($GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#TempB) & "_is"), 1))) & " of " & $Name(#TempC) & "'s controls so your challenge was automatically ended."\par
Else\par
/SendPM #TempC, $BotName & ": " & $Name(#TempB) & " is violating " & $Str(#TempD) & " out of " & $Str(#Val($Right($GetValue("The_PSID_of_" & $Name(#TempB) & "_is"), 1))) & " of your controls so the challenge was automatically ended."\par
EndIf\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB = #Source\par
/Set #TempB, #Target\par
/Set #TempC, #Source\par
/Set #TempD, 1\par
/Set #TempF, 1\par
/Set #TempE, 0\par
GoTo Controls\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If $Right($TempA,1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Target) & "'s RPG Status is Off."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #GetCompat(#Source) <> 5 AND #GetCompat(#Source) <> 6 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You need to be 'Full Advanced' OR 'Modded Database' in your team."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #GetCompat(#Target) <> 5 AND #GetCompat(#Target) <> 6 \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your opponent needs to have a 'Full Advanced' OR 'Modded Database' team."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Target,PSID) & "_RPGStats")\par
If #GL(#Source) > 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Gym Leader's can't challenge."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #GL(#Target) > 0\par
If #Valid(#Target) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": The Gym Leader is not accepting challenges at the moment."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Team(#Source) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not full so you still have to capture more Pok\'e9mon before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Valid(#Source) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not valid so you still have to make sure your team match our records before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Mid($Message, 5, 1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Gym Leaders only use stadium mode."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:ChallengeList\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp)) <> ""\par
If $GetValue("TName_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp))) = $Name(#Source)\par
:DelChallenge\par
/SaveValue "Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp), ""\par
If $GetValue("TName_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp+1))) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp), $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp+1))\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo DelChallenge\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp)))) > 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $GetValue("Gym_" & $Str(#GL(#Target)) & "_LeadChal_" & $Str(#Temp))) & " is on the server and his/her name is above you on the Gym Leader's Challenge List."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
GoTo ChallengeList\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": You have never signed up to challenge this Gym Leader in the first place."\par
EndIf\par
If #GL(#Target) = 28 OR #GL(#Target) = 23\par
/SendPM #Target, $RPGBotName & ": Before accepting the challenge make sure it is a Double Battle."\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($Temp,1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not initialized yet so you can't battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If $Left($TempA,1) = "0"\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Target) & "'s Team is not initialized yet so s/he can't battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Team(#Source) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not full so you still have to capture more Pok\'e9mon before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Valid(#Source) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": Your team is not Valid so you still have to make sure your team match our records before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Team(#Target) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Target) & "'s Team is not full so they still have to capture more Pok\'e9mon before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Valid(#Target) = 0\par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Target) & "'s Team is not valid so they still have to make sure your team match our records before you can battle."\par
/StopEvent\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par
\par
Event -BattleBegin\par
If $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_ChampionShip") <> "" AND $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Target,PSID) & "_ChampionShip") <> ""\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID) & "_ChampionShip") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($GetPlayerInfo(#Target,PSID) & "_ChampionShip")\par
If $Mid($Temp, 5, 1) = $Mid($TempA, 5, 1) AND $Mid($Temp, 4, 1) = $Mid($TempA, 4, 1) AND $Mid($TempA, 4, 1) = "1" AND $Right($Temp, 2) = $Right($TempA, 2) AND $Left($Temp, 1) = $Left($TempA, 1) \par
/SendPM #Source, $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " and " & $Name(#Target) & " are starting a " & $GetValue("Champ_" & $Left($Temp, 1)) & " Championship's Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Mid($TempA, 5, 1) & " Match!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\par
\par
Event -BattleOver\par
If #IsLoaded(#Target) = 0 AND #IsLoaded(#Source) = 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #IsLoaded(#Target) = 0 \par
/Set $TempG, $Opponent(#Source)\par
Else\par
/Set $TempG, $GetPlayerInfo(#Target,PSID)\par
EndIf\par
If #IsLoaded(#Source) = 0 \par
/Set $TempH, $Opponent(#Target)\par
Else\par
/Set $TempH, $GetPlayerInfo(#Source,PSID)\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue($TempH & "_ChampionShip") <> "" AND $GetValue($TempG & "_ChampionShip") <> ""\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempH & "_ChampionShip") \par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($TempG & "_ChampionShip")\par
If $Mid($Temp, 5, 1) = $Mid($TempA, 5, 1) AND $Mid($Temp, 4, 1) = $Mid($TempA, 4, 1) AND $Mid($TempA, 4, 1) = "1" AND $Right($Temp, 2) = $Right($TempA, 2) AND $Left($Temp, 1) = $Left($TempA, 1) \par
If #IsIn($Message,"TIE") > 0\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": A tie has taken place! A rematch is required!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Right($Temp, 2))\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Mid($Temp, 4, 1))\par
/Inc #CSMems, - 1\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempA) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp), $Mid($Temp, 2, 2)\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempA) & "_Mem", #GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempA) & "_Mem") - 1\par
/SaveValue $TempG & "_ChampionShip", \f1 $Left($TempA, 3) & "3" & $Mid($TempA, 5, 1) & "00"\f0\par
/SaveValue $TempH & "_ChampionShip", $Left($Temp, 3) & "2" \f1 & \f0 $Right($Temp, 3)\par
/SendAll $RPGBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " has qualified for the next round!"\par
/Set #TempB, #TempA\par
GoTo CSR\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Tourney > 1 AND #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMems"),$TempH) > 0 AND #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMems"),$TempG) > 0\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempH)\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempG)\par
If #Val($Mid($Temp, 5, 2)) = #Val($Mid($TempA, 5, 2)) AND #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 5, 2)))), "-") > 0\par
If #IsIn($Message,"TIE") > 0\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A tie has taken place! A rematch is required!"\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Val($Mid($Temp, 5, 2))\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp), $Left($Temp,2)\par
/Inc #TourneyMems, - 1\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempG, $Left($TempA, 3) & "300"\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempH, $Left($Temp, 3) & "2" & $Right($Temp, 2)\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": " & $Name(#Source) & " has qualified for the next round!"\par
GoTo RoundCheck\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, $TournBotName & ": This was not Tournament Match!"\par
/SendPM #Target, $TournBotName & ": This was not Tournament Match!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo Skip\par
:CSR\par
\f1 /Set #Temp, 1\par
:CSRound\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)),"-") > 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo CSRound\par
EndIf\f0\par
\f1 If #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 )) = 1\par
\f0 /Set $Temp, $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))\par
/Set $TempB, \f1 $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_1")\f0\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
\f1 /SendAll ""\par
\f0 /SendAll "*** " & $UCASE($GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round Announcement") & " ***"\par
\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " has just passed the " & \f0 $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & ", Congratulations!"\par
\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": Now " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " faces the infamous Elite 4!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
\f0 /SaveValue $TempA & "_ChampionShip", $Left($GetValue($TempA & "_ChampionShip"), 3) & "4" & $Mid($GetValue($TempA & "_ChampionShip"), 5, 1) & "01"\f1\par
\f0 /SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round", "A"\par
\f1 /Exit\par
Else\par
\f0 /SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round", \f1 #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Round"\f1 )) + 1\f0\par
\f1 /SendAll ""\par
\f0 /SendAll "*** " & $UCASE($GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round Announcement") & " ***"\par
\f1 /SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": The " & \f0 $GetValue("Champ_" & $Str(#Temp)) & " Championship Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & " \f1 has just entered Round " & $Str(#Tourney-1) & "!"\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": There are " & $GetValue(\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Mem"\f1 ) & " members who are still in the \f0 Preliminary Round's Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & " \f1 out of " & $GetValue(\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Max"\f1 ) & " players!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:CSVal\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right("0" & $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)), 2) & ","\par
If #Temp < #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo CSVal\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:DelCS\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If $GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), ""\par
If #TempA < 8\par
GoTo DelCS\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, \f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))\f1\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": Randomizing \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Brackets......."\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:RandomCS\par
/Set #TempC, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($TempC,(#TempC*2) + (#TempC-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempA & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set #TempC, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempC,(#TempC*2) + (#TempC-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempB & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempA)*21) + (#Val($TempA)-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), $TempB & "-" & $TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match", #TempA\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue($TempD & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempD & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue($TempE & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempE & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
If #Temp > 1\par
GoTo RandomCS\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": A random player is given a Bye to the next round because of the lack of an opponent!"\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($TempC,2)\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Left($TempC,2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempC*21) + (#TempC-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue($TempA & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 )\par
/SaveValue $TempA & "_\f0 ChampionShip"\f1 , $Left($TempB, 3) & "2" & $Mid($TempF, 5, 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2) \par
/SaveValue "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match", #TempA\par
EndIf\par
/Set #SendCS, 0\par
GoTo CSBracket\par
:CSBracket\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Bracket listings are as follows."\par
Else\par
/SendAll $\f0 RPGBotName \f1 & ": \f0 Preliminary Round Tier " & $Str(#TempB) & "\f1  Match Bracket listings are as follows..."\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, \f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB))\f1\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:CSMatchShow\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)), "-") > 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set #TempC, #Val($Right($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21)+(#TempA-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp,(#TempC*21)+(#TempC-21),21)\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)\par
EndIf\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)) = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)\par
EndIf\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($GetValue("ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match_" & $Str(#Temp)))\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21)) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))\par
EndIf\par
If #SendCS = 1\par
/SendPM #Source, "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
Else\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #Val(\f0 $GetValue\f1 (\f0 "ChampBracket_" & $Str(#TempB) & "_Match"\f1 ))\par
GoTo CSMatchShow\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB < 4\par
GoTo \f0 OBOReturn\f1\par
\f0 EndIf\f1\par
If #SendCS = 0\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
Else\par
/SendPM #Source, ""\par
EndIf\par
/Exit\f0\par
:RoundCheck\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:Round\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),"-") > 0\par
/Exit\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo Round\par
EndIf\par
If #TourneyMatch = 1\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TourneyMatch_1")\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": " & $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & " has just won the " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament, Congratulations!"\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("The_TPoints_of_" & $TempA & "_are")\par
/SaveValue "The_TPoints_of_" & $TempA & "_are", $Left($Temp, (#TourneyType * 2) - 2) & $Right("00" & $Str(#Val($Mid($Temp, (#TourneyType * 2) - 1, 2)) + 1), 2) & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - (#TourneyType * 2))\par
/SendPM #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)), $BotName & ": You earned 25 Tokens!"\par
/SaveValue $TempA & "_Tokens", #GetValue($TempA & "_Tokens") + 25\par
/Set #Tourney, 0\par
/Exit\par
Else\par
/Inc #Tourney\par
/SendAll ""\par
/SendAll "*** " & $UCASE("Tournament Announcement") & " ***"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": The " & $GetValue("Tourney_" & $Str(#TourneyType)) & " Tournament has just entered Round " & $Str(#Tourney-1) & "!"\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": There are " & $Str(#TourneyMems) & " members who are still in the Tournament out of " & $Str(#TourneyMax) & " players!"\par
/Set $TempC, ""\par
/Set #Temp, 1\par
:WinVal\par
/Set $TempC, $TempC & $Right("0" &$GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)), 2) & ","\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
/Inc #Temp\par
GoTo WinVal\par
EndIf\par
/Set #Temp, #TourneyMatch\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:Dele\par
/Inc #TempA\par
If $GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA)) <> ""\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), ""\par
If #TempA < 32\par
GoTo Dele\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Randomizing Tournament Match Brackets ......."\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:RandomMatch\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempA & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set #TempB, #Rand(#Temp,1)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*2) + (#TempB-2),2)\par
/Set $TempC, $Replace($TempC, $TempB & ",", "")\par
/Inc #Temp, -1\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempA)*21) + (#Val($TempA)-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempE, $Mid($Temp, (#Val($TempB)*21) + (#Val($TempB)-21), 21)\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $TempB & "-" & $TempA\par
/Set #TourneyMatch, #TempA\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempD)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempD, $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
/Set $TempF, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempE)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempE, $Left($TempF, 3) & "1" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2)\par
If #Temp > 1\par
GoTo RandomMatch\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = 1\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": A random player is given a Bye to the next round because of the lack of an opponent!"\par
/Inc #TempA\par
/SaveValue "TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#TempA), $Left($TempC,2)\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Left($TempC,2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp, (#TempB*21) + (#TempB-21), 21)\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TStats_" & $TempA)\par
/SaveValue "TStats_" & $TempA, $Left($TempB, 3) & "2" & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempA),2) \par
/Set #TourneyMatch, #TempA\par
EndIf\par
GoTo ShowBracket\par
:ShowBracket\par
/SendAll $TournBotName & ": Match bracket listings are as follows..."\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue("TourneyMems")\par
/Set #Temp, 0\par
:TourneyMatchShow\par
/Inc #Temp\par
If #IsIn($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)), "-") > 0\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($Left($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set #TempB, #Val($Right($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)),2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21)+(#TempA-21),21)\par
/Set $TempB, $Mid($Temp,(#TempB*21)+(#TempB-21),21)\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempA)\par
EndIf\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)) = 0\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $GetValue("TName_" & $TempB)\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " vs " & $TempB & "!"\par
Else\par
/Set #TempA, #Val($GetValue("TourneyMatch_" & $Str(#Temp)))\par
If #PNumber($GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))) = 0\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21)) & "[Absent]"\par
Else\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue("TName_" & $Mid($Temp,(#TempA*21) + (#TempA-21),21))\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "Match" & $Str(#Temp) & ": " & $TempA & " is qualified for the next round!"\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp < #TourneyMatch\par
GoTo TourneyMatchShow\par
EndIf\par
/SendAll "*** ******************************************* ***"\par
/SendAll ""\par
/Exit\par

/SendPM #Temp, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#TempC) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Str(#TempC)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempI & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, (#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45)  + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempC, $GetValue($TempI & "_PokesLove")\par
/Set $TempD, $Mid($TempC,(#TempB*7) + (#TempB-7),7)\par
If #Val($Right($TempD, 2)) > 18\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_0") > 0 OR $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_1") > 0 OR $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_2") > 0 \par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_1") > 0\par
If #DayT > 5 AND #Day = 2 OR #DayT < 2 AND #Day = 1\par
GoTo NotLoveEvo\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempC, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_1")\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_2") > 0\par
If #DayT > 9 AND #Day = 1 OR #DayT < 6 AND #Day = 2\par
GoTo NotLoveEvo\par
EndIf\par
/Set #TempC, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_2")\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, #GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA,3))) & "_Love_0")\par
EndIf\par
/SendPM #Temp, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#TempC) & "!"\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $Str(#TempC), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempI & "_Pokes")\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, (#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
:NotLoveEvo\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/SendPM #Temp, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to learn the move " & $Move(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3))))) & "!"\par
/Set #TempC, 7\par
:PokeEvoMove\par
If #TempC < 14\par
If $Mid($TempB,#TempC,3) <> "000"\par
/Inc #TempC, + 3\par
GoTo PokeEvoMove\par
EndIf\par
Else\par
/Set #TempC, 7\par
EndIf\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB, #TempC - 1) & $Right("00" & $Str(#GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Lv_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3))))), 3) & $Right($TempB,#Len($TempB) - (#TempC + 2))\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, (#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
EndIf\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To") <> ""\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, (#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Temp, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "!"\par
Else\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To") <> ""\par
If $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)))) <> ""\par
/Set $TempB, $Left($TempB,15) & $Right("00" & $GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To"), 3)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp,(#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Temp, "*** Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " is trying to evolve into "  & $Pokemon(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($GetValue("Poke_" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "_Evo_To"))) & "!"\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
GoTo LevelGrow\par
Else\par
/Set $TempB, $Right("00000" & $Str(#Val($Left($TempB, 6)) - #TempI), 6) & $Right($TempB, #Len($TempB) - 6)\par
/Set $TempA, $Left($TempA, #Len($TempA) - 18) & $TempB\par
/Set $Temp, $Left($Temp, (#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) - 1) & $TempA & $Right($Temp, #Len($Temp) - ((#TempB * 45) + (#TempB - 45) + 44))\par
/SaveValue $TempI & "_Pokes", $Temp\par
/SendPM #Temp, $RPGBotName & ": Your " & $Pokemon(#Val($Left($TempA, 3))) & " needs " & $Str(#Val($Left($TempB,6))) & " experience points to grow to Lv" & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempA, 4, 3)) + 1) & "!"\par
EndIf\par
If #TempB < 6 \par
GoTo Experience\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = #Source\par
If $Right($TempC, 1) <> "1"\par
/Set #TempC, #Temp\par
/Set #Temp, #TempA\par
/Set #TempA, #TempC\par
/Set #TempB, 0\par
/Set $TempI, $TempG\par
GoTo Experience\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
/Set $Temp, $GetValue($TempH & "_RPGStats")\par
/Set $TempA, $GetValue($TempG & "_RPGStats")\par
/Set #Temp, #Source\par
/Set #TempA, 0\par
:NewInfo\par
/Set $TempC, $Temp\par
If #IsLoaded(#Temp) = 1 AND #IsIn($GetValue("AllGLs"), "," & $Name(#Temp) & ",") = 0\par
/Set #Cash(#Temp), #Val($Mid($TempC, 6, 6))\par
/Set #Health(#Temp), #Val($Mid($TempC, 3, 3))\par
/Set $Extrinfo(#Temp), " LifePoints: " & $Str(#Health(#Temp)) & " | Area: " & $Area(#Temp) & " | Badges: " & $Str(#Val($Mid($TempC, 12, 2))) & " | Cash: $" & $Str(#Cash(#Temp)) & "]." & $OrigEXTR(#Temp)\par
If $Name(#Temp) = "Mew Master" OR $Name(#Temp) = "Lord Meshadieme" OR $Name(#Temp) = "Lamel"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Temp, EXTR, "[Creator of this RPG - " & $Extrinfo(#Temp)\par
Else \par
If $Name(#Temp) = "Bikaben"\par
/SetPlayerInfo #Temp, EXTR, "[Host of this RPG - " & $Extrinfo(#Temp) \par
Else \par
/SetPlayerInfo #Temp, EXTR, "[Mew's RPG Player - " & $Extrinfo(#Temp) \par
EndIf \par
EndIf\par
/Set $NewEXTR(#Temp), $GetPlayerInfo(#Temp, EXTR)\par
EndIf\par
If #Temp = #Source\par
/Set #Temp, #Target\par
/Set $TempC, $TempA\par
/Set $TempI, $TempG\par
GoTo NewInfo\par
EndIf\par
EndIf\par
EndEvent\f2\fs20\par
}
